
-----title
阳新 (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1140')">1136-1140年</a>　少年居家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1149')">1141-1149年</a>　在永兴读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在兴国军学读书，举秀才。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1156')">1151-1156年</a>　在兴国军学读书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2e63062fc79541e7b9e693619df1098f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2e63062fc79541e7b9e693619df1098f");'><span id='2e63062fc79541e7b9e693619df1098f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1166')">1164-1166年</a>，30-32岁</div><div id='2e63062fc79541e7b9e693619df1098f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年9月</a>　罢太学正后离京回兴国，友人陆游送别，王阮亦寄诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年9月</a>　居兴国，应郡守张采之请，作太守题名记。作品：《兴国太守题名记》<div id='poem_1274143' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274143' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274143?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴国太守题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274143")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274143_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274143'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274143'>荥阳张公采元亮为此郡，无毫发不称人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274143_comment'></div>郡阙太守题名，元亮心不满之，间谓某曰：「前事之不忘，后事之师也，去者漫然，来何观焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274143_comment'></div>不惟如是，太守于民有父母之道、师帅之义，行路视之，人情薄哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274143_comment'></div>顾有所不决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274143_comment'></div>江西一道十馀州，此最毒于兵，凡图书金石皆散坏不可稽验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274143_comment'></div>我最后于诸公，故老遗黎日就彫零，益无所咨叩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274143_comment'></div>数熙、丰来杨公绘、王公琪各以文章事业表见，李公宜又捍难保门，有即墨平原之功，至于今诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274143_comment'></div>然追其岁纪官称，已莫获其详，姑凭其概见著之，惧有舛焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274143_comment'></div>独得王公敷以次实之，将于此乎权舆，阙者夥矣，如之何而可」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274143_comment'></div>质曰：「著而舛犹未著也，疑者于法从阙，又何尤焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274143_comment'></div>于是始定于王公敷，凡若干人，具次于左方。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1274143_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　期间，与张采有诗唱和。作品：《张元亮见访留和坐客》《起伏龙行呈张元亮》<div id='poem_548832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张元亮见访留和坐客</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548832")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548832'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548832'>杯盘仓卒但随家，所赖龙山得孟嘉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548832'>略以诗声知律吕，敢于学海望津涯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548832'>精神霜后千头橘，风味新时一颗瓜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548832'>发白未应馀子识，汗青当有后人誇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548832_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548832'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548832_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>起伏龙行呈张元亮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1164年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548718")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548718_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548718'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548718'>使君寸丹通九渊，冷彻龙胆惊不眠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548718'>掣关稽首玉帝前，青霓影里一粲鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548718'>群龙下走如奔泉，电旗掀舞雷车旋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548718'>怒蛟腾起缠阴涎，四海五湖归一髯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548718'>黄尘白沙飞满川，顷刻变作声潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548718'>何人此手有此拳，敛散风雨麾云烟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548718'>一州千里十万廛，翻覆歉岁为丰年。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548718'>云花缭绕金连钱，使君倚鞚将朝天。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548718'>千珠万玉倾箱圆，夕阳扪腹秋风边。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548718'>此时可怀不可瞻，何不留取黄金鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548718'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_548718_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　居兴国，应兴国守张采之请，作《汪参政生祠堂记》<div id='poem_1274144' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274144' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274144?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汪参政生祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274144")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274144_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274144'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274144'>绍兴三十一年秋七月，诏以御史中丞鄱阳汪公宣谕荆襄，自行都及襄阳，所过搜疵剔隐，凡格而不流与壅而不上达者，咸驿置以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274144_comment'></div>天子惟公为信，疏函朝通，膏泽夕下，而兴国被惠最厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274144_comment'></div>兴国地多山谷，其稍夷衍者则漫为深潴浅泽，不得尽为民资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274144_comment'></div>又当江淮走集之冲，往尝与东南巨寇桀贼为巢窟，蹂躏戕圮，较一道十州独甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274144_comment'></div>旧占籍八万四千九百有奇，今二万三千六百有奇，是存者四之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274144_comment'></div>旧输苗六万一千有奇，今三万二千七百有奇，是损者十之五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274144_comment'></div>以四一之民输十五之租，其他称是，已不可复任，而淮衣与税缣并征，税缣四千有奇，淮衣六千三百有奇，垂将倍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274144_comment'></div>公且至，众相谋曰：「被此毒以来，叩郡庭，凑使台，谒省闼，先后以数十计矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274144_comment'></div>朝廷取决于民部，民部有司也，奚敢议绳尺之外？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274144_comment'></div>故屡进弗获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274144_comment'></div>今天子寄公耳目心腹，公又聪明果达，祥顺慈厚，与天子意相通，试告之，宜纳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274144_comment'></div>既至，相率群拜于庭，列次于门，且延于衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274144_comment'></div>千人一色，惨怛怵惕，久乃得言曰：「维氓幸生兹时，还定安集，尚敢冀其他！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274144_comment'></div>惟是淮衣沿袭因循，遂成不革，灼烂肌肤，灰灭头颅，于今有年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274144_comment'></div>愿假须臾之景，有请于公」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274144_comment'></div>公曰：「何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274144_comment'></div>吾惟有不知，知之敢有不告天子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274144_comment'></div>惟有不知，知之岂有弗行！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274144_comment'></div>尔其示我以详」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274144_comment'></div>于是进曰：「初，大河未他裂，郡有赋曰黄河卷埽钱，缗计一万七千有奇，蕲、黄为代输，而郡以缣充之，匹计一万四千有奇，自大观二年始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274144_comment'></div>今黄河不卷埽，蕲、黄不代输，而淮衣著为经常，自绍兴五年始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274144_comment'></div>其初二千一百有奇，二十五年增六千三百有奇，及大观之数则止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274144_comment'></div>膏竭命殚，可以损不可以加，公其哀之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274144_comment'></div>公应曰：「诺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274144_comment'></div>又进曰：「往者以钱视缣，缗计一百二十有奇得缣百，承平时其直相当，民虽不欲而犹能堪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274144_comment'></div>今无易缣之钱，而一缣之估钱四千五百有奇，是一缣而羡三倍之钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274144_comment'></div>往者蕲、黄与兴国各有亏馀相通，蕲、黄为兴国供河埽，兴国为蕲、黄调省缣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274144_comment'></div>今蕲、黄自若，而兴国独抱虚逋承实祸，是一州而输三郡之赋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274144_comment'></div>公又应曰：「诺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274144_comment'></div>明年春正月，公归，拜参知政事，具白其事，天子即诏有司以为率勿增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274144_comment'></div>令下，阖一郡三邑数万之生灵扶伏踊跃，首击地，手加额，上戴天子，次则戴公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274144_comment'></div>维天子高视两仪万物之上，敝屣神器，褰裳遗之，何藻色之可状而端倪之可窥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274144_comment'></div>公出而与世同忧，公不能忘世，世亦不能忘公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274144_comment'></div>众又相谋曰：「古者敬爱其人而不得亲，或思其人而无所寄情，则貌而奉之，故其像有画，其祠有堂」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274144_comment'></div>于是乡党喜事有力者相与述人情，规古义，以请于太守张公采，太守曰：「地庳薄则不称位，宇嚣隘则不称德，画得其略而不得其详则不称容」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274144_comment'></div>乃得西城佛宫，相其位置之尤者杰为之屋，而择其辈行之名者工为之貌，奔走经营，无所不用其至，而后得公精神仪干，冠冕佩服之真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274144_comment'></div>既具，以晓其部之民，民曰：「如是可以无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274144_comment'></div>虽然，自辛及乙，宿师用兵五年，沟池棹舰楼橹营屯之役，金铁丝纩谷粟皮羽之敛，鱼鳞鸟氄错布叠出，呜呼殆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274144_comment'></div>斯民岌岌乎此邦也，淮衣至是亦将无以为输，且朝廷知其无名，盍亦除之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274144_comment'></div>吾侪小人苦不知足之嘲，愿受而不避，无亦使盛世清朝，何有待来年之云」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274144_comment'></div>太守曰：「天子视民如伤，公爱物如己，千载一遇，不谋而同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274144_comment'></div>公将秉执元钧，佐佑太平，兵甲敛息，无所兴发，府库充仞，无所庀藏，复常庸，蠲常租，省常调，尔行将见之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274144_comment'></div>民曰：「如是诚可以无憾」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1274144_comment'></div>则以告其客汶阳王质，求文以列实，质不敢辞，不独以彰天子之圣，著公之贤，凡志士仁人皆可以动心焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1274144_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　友人李处全罢后权发遣知沅州。途经兴国军，与王质聚首，有诗唱和。作品：《和李粹伯》<div id='poem_548873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和李粹伯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548873")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548873'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548873'>不多风雨已秋容，惨澹斜阳湿晚红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548873'>长忆蘋风过归雁，更思烟浪拍垂虹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548873'>未应堂上烛能灭，所愿樽中酒不空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548873'>卷雪楼前卸帆日，却从天际望吴中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548873'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年</a>　友人李处全在兴国聚首，有诗唱和。作品：《又和李粹伯》<div id='poem_548874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又和李粹伯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1165年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548874")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548874'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548874'>云似诸公簿领閒，不名阿堵但江山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548874'>秋风未白平生发，尊酒聊赪壮士颜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548874'>醉后参虚无咫尺，悲来天地总间关。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548874'>归眠梦绕潇湘野，红叶黄花满望斑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548874_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548874'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年8月26日</a>　秋，起复任国子正。赴任前，八月二十六日王十朋来会于兴国，有诗唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年7月</a>　在国子正任上，七月罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　罢后重回兴国。是秋，太守张采将去任，作《去思楼记》<div id='poem_1274145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274145' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274145?labeling=true' target='_blank'>去思楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274145")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274145_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274145'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274145'>兴国太守张公未去郡之三月，作南门，冠楼于其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274145_comment'></div>通守王君澬间语余曰：「楼将成，名未具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274145_comment'></div>此邦人民心不负于公之去，而力不足于公之留，有怏怏不满之容，有郁郁嗟吟之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274145_comment'></div>夫未去而惜，则既去而思也不既切乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274145_comment'></div>吾以去思名之，人情宜，事实称也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274145_comment'></div>余曰：今之为吏，与古异也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274145_comment'></div>不论古，与往数年，又异也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274145_comment'></div>不论数年，与往十馀年，又异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274145_comment'></div>古者事省而易应，法简而易行，物丰而易征，人醇而易令，故吏之为力也易施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274145_comment'></div>长老所传，承平未乱之时，虽拙者犹能从容閒暇，有办而无趣，退食之馀，赏心乐事，销太平之景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274145_comment'></div>以余所见，距此三数年，太守亦或閒庭几而府库仓廪闻其充，未闻其竭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274145_comment'></div>有时而竭，亦有时而充，未闻其不可复充也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274145_comment'></div>独八九年来，为吏者至不可终朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274145_comment'></div>余往来兵间，所历殆遍东南，平时丰州壮县，气象变改，月异而岁不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274145_comment'></div>诸公所忧，方隅乏佳政之吏，田野少欢声之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274145_comment'></div>此亦何足怪也，事益繁，法益急，物益窘，人益浇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274145_comment'></div>御益浇之人，掊益窘之物，守益急之法，应益繁之事，虽黄霸、龚遂、卓茂、鲁恭之贤，将施其所积而遂其欲，不独余知其难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274145_comment'></div>民不能以尽徇吏，故吏之怨民日深，吏不能以尽假民，故民之雠吏日毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274145_comment'></div>当是之时，有未去而怨者矣，乌有既去而思者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274145_comment'></div>而张公所遇，又天下之至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274145_comment'></div>建炎、绍兴之交，江西无地无兵，而兴国受毒最酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274145_comment'></div>旧占籍八万四千九百有奇，今二万三千六百有奇，是存者四之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274145_comment'></div>旧秋输六万一千有奇，今三万二千七百有奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274145_comment'></div>夏输十一万三千九百有奇，今五万七千一百有奇，是损者十之五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274145_comment'></div>以四一之民输十五之租，而又无故输淮衣六千三百有奇，难解兵二十馀年，益困弗苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274145_comment'></div>而辛巳至于甲申，复连兵四年，沟池棹舰楼橹营屯之役，金铁丝纩弓甲皮羽之敛，视大州同科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274145_comment'></div>而以和为籴者少亦不下五千有奇，以汰去军者多，稍增至一百有奇，大州不堪，而况于兴国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274145_comment'></div>公来以甲申之夏，其去以丙戌之秋，经大役者二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274145_comment'></div>兴国平居为盗贼之渊，甲申之虞，猺毒垂发，公猎取数辈，亟惨治之而警其馀，奸不得肆，民乃少定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274145_comment'></div>凡城之隅若江之濒布民兵，其冲远者敕吏调，存抚视，近辄自行炽薪𭶢酒，躬酌以饮民，博飧巨胾佐之，部勒卒乘，整厉弓戈，出入游警，以张民兵之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274145_comment'></div>行者归，居者安，强者奋，弱者不恐，市无欢言，野无走尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274145_comment'></div>若贫若富，相安以卒无事，故警既撤而民始亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274145_comment'></div>乙酉合忠义新军于江州，露食草宿，立须具庐，兴国当三百有奇，为木若竹若芦若铁十万有奇，伐削之工、覆筑之工、建治之工、迁运之工，举不在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274145_comment'></div>欢讹相惊，欲遁欲移，不能者含忧以俟毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274145_comment'></div>已而一物以计皆赋资于民而易其物，一工以积皆假直于民而取其工，凡物视其时之价，凡工视其私之佣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274145_comment'></div>内郭外郊，奔冲衔属，而乐与之从事，既周其身，又濡其家，故役既已而民益爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274145_comment'></div>以再岁考之，上供之运钱计十万五千有奇，米计十二万三千有奇，吏兵之俸钱计五万七千有奇，米计八万四千有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274145_comment'></div>至陋之国，极困之民，然而财以时输上，上不绳愆，俸以时给下，下不告病，此宜其度越经常，酝酿新奇，有所不免者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274145_comment'></div>问之在廛，在廛不知，问之在野，在野不知，余能言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274145_comment'></div>穷其微眇而塞其漏，钳其变态而销其奸，析其奇赢而啬其出，严其开阖而谨其藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274145_comment'></div>如苦儒专经，穷昼夜之力，争尺寸之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274145_comment'></div>如枯僧缚禅，弃形体寝食于寒暑之外，拾遗腐于粪壤之聚，夺掩匿于盗贼之怀，故财纾于上而赋不及于下，劳切于身而扰不至于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274145_comment'></div>自公观之，以身之劳易民之扰，自民观之，移己之痛为他人之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1274145_comment'></div>此而不有所感，禽鱼无此情，蛮貊无此理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1274145_comment'></div>则未去而惜，既去而思，何异之足言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1274145_comment'></div>而余独念夫当故人难施巧之时，处今人至不幸之地，去而得思于民，此不亦天下之至难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1274145_comment'></div>或者不以余言为然，自履之则知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1274145_comment'></div>故余之于公惟怜其至难，而叹其不可能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1274145_comment'></div>公名采，字元亮，郑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1274145_comment'></div>是为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1274145_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4da35a7409b64467bdc262f272b8e4ad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4da35a7409b64467bdc262f272b8e4ad");'><span id='4da35a7409b64467bdc262f272b8e4ad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>，33岁</div><div id='4da35a7409b64467bdc262f272b8e4ad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年6月</a>　六月，虞允文宣抚川陕，辟质偕行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年闰7月</a>　闰七月，代虞允文作慰问表。作品：《代慰安恭皇后祔庙表》<div id='poem_1274087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代慰安恭皇后祔庙表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年闰7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274087")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274087'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274087'>升驭于天，莫瞻柔范；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274087_comment'></div>妥灵于庙，永閟徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274087_comment'></div>共衔厚载之恩，益结无穷之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274087_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下道隆正始，德茂齐家，忽彫婺宿之辉，遽失坤舆之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274087_comment'></div>虽瑶池之燕方适，难回王母之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274087_comment'></div>然《关雎》之应已成，无损《周南》之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274087_comment'></div>愿宽哀抱，俯慰群情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1274087_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年闰7月11日</a>　十一日，自兴国启程由陆路入川。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='51a7513eb6394d13a9b304df9e25ef01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("51a7513eb6394d13a9b304df9e25ef01");'><span id='51a7513eb6394d13a9b304df9e25ef01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，35岁</div><div id='51a7513eb6394d13a9b304df9e25ef01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年4月10日</a>　四月十日至兴国，此行累八十日。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年6月</a>　六月张孝祥卒，有诗哀悼。作品：《忆张安国》<div id='poem_548816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆张安国</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548816")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548816'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548816'>天上足官府，舍人何处归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548816'>世情伤幻化，道眼羡空飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548816'>易合谁终始，难言有是非。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548816'>九原如可作，来共立斜晖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548816_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548816'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548816_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年6月</a>　六月张孝祥卒，有词哀悼。作品：《八声甘州（怀张安国）》<div id='poem_73004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_73004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/73004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八声甘州<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>怀张安国</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_73004")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_73004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_73004'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_73004'>海茫茫、天北与天南，吾友定安归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_73004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_73004'>闻濡须江上，皖公山下，驾白云飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_73004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73004'>莽苍空郊虚野，古路立斜晖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_73004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73004'>颜蹠皆尘土，苦泪休挥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73004_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_73004'>一代锦肠绣肺，想英魂皎皎，健口霏霏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_73004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_73004'>望寒空明月，无路寄相思。<div id='poem_sentence_5_73004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_73004'>叹千古、兴亡成败，满乾坤、遗恨有谁知。<div id='poem_sentence_6_73004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_73004'>今何在，一川烟惨，万壑风悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_73004_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年10月19日</a>　十月，又因晁公武辟入幕，自兴国再入成都。友人李流谦有诗相送。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a6c08d123e234b2c8419506b843106f8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a6c08d123e234b2c8419506b843106f8");'><span id='a6c08d123e234b2c8419506b843106f8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>，36岁</div><div id='a6c08d123e234b2c8419506b843106f8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年8月1日</a>　八月一日到兴国，又有书信寄虞允文。作品：《与虞相书》（二）<div id='poem_1274096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274096' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274096?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与虞相书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274096")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274096'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274096'>某伏以即日凛秋，恭惟一德享天，万年永相，钧候起居万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274096_comment'></div>某乃七月二十日以书彻于相公，时则在武昌，今八月一日以书达于相公，时则在兴国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274096_comment'></div>入蜀半期而无一字出蜀，一旬而致二缄，有嫌无嫌之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274096_comment'></div>某之作蜀，视景偷生，杜门避死之不给，矧敢通宰执之讯，以重危疑之嫌哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274096_comment'></div>相公可以嘿喻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274096_comment'></div>今以父子迫切之情，虽有嫌且不惮，况无嫌乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274096_comment'></div>伏念家君好古专经，老犹不倦，居家临官，介然自守，其勤畏廉纯异常，虽当世独行立节之士未易及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274096_comment'></div>惟是屈于不遇之命，少困场屋，老沈下僚，虽家君处之夷然，而为子之职当无所不用其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274096_comment'></div>今夷陵之掾垂满，异时之计不知所以裁之，涉数千里而调官，固非老者所宜，待三五年而得禄，又非贫者所能守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274096_comment'></div>私窃自念，某省罢在法所优而一等差遣，在朝廷所当予而难却者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274096_comment'></div>今同官王亢子苍自干办而升治中，省罢不一月而被命到官，未十日而获迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274096_comment'></div>此虽非某孤寒懒退者所当援以为例，而议者不能无羡亢而嗟某也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274096_comment'></div>伏睹朝廷均视亲疏，决无彼此，愿以所当得而移之于亲，此亦朝廷所乐为而易从，足以厚风俗而非启侥倖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274096_comment'></div>具在别牍，敢蕲鸿造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274096_comment'></div>某之自视良亦甚明，固有欲抑之者矣，安在其为抑之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274096_comment'></div>梁武帝作浮山堰遏长淮以灌北道，或曰四渎天所以宣泄其气，不可塞也，浮山一败而淮南皆海矣，故人之负英气与物之抱俊具者皆不可抑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274096_comment'></div>吕夷简抑群贤而庆历之党论兴，王安石抑群贤而元祐、绍圣之党事炽，蔡京抑群贤而宣和、靖康之党祸极矣，故不可抑而抑之，抑者受名，抑之者受谤，甚则受祸，岂不悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274096_comment'></div>孙沔上封事诋吕夷简，以柔而易制者升为心腹，以奸而可使者任为羽翼，不进贤才，但用不如己者，自为之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274096_comment'></div>仁宗遣中使持书即第示之，夷简读而叹曰：「善哉，元规之言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274096_comment'></div>恨不早闻十年耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274096_comment'></div>盖申公是时逼老将退，虽知悔已无及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274096_comment'></div>惜莆田丞相之在位未尝闻斯言也，今虽去矣，尚可告之，庶有济哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274096_comment'></div>相公恢宏洪博善与人同，天下所以系望而知归者以相公之大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274096_comment'></div>文潞公欲引恬退之士，谋于其客张子平，潞公曰：「宜莫如韩维、张瑰也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274096_comment'></div>子平曰：「王安石以静退著名，其可遗乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274096_comment'></div>潞公不答，子平曰：「岂以瑰事相公加勤，而安石无所加乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274096_comment'></div>潞公瞿然，乃并荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274096_comment'></div>愿相公勿以事我之疏数为轻重，则天下之贤无遗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274096_comment'></div>王文公数荐寇莱公，真宗曰：「准屡言卿过，而卿力荐之，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274096_comment'></div>文正曰：「臣备位宰辅，政事多阙，他人相顾不言，准独能攻臣之短，纳忠陛下，此乃臣所以重准也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274096_comment'></div>愿陛下亟用之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274096_comment'></div>愿相公勿以于我有毁誉而为去取，则天下之贤归心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274096_comment'></div>今某乃独以龌龊而不能有所开拓取人主之轻，受天下之责，则相公可不辟至公之路、开众正之门，上广天子蒐揽贤豪之心，下恢士大夫驰骛当世之气哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274096_comment'></div>某此生永已，无路报恩，惟望相公以道事君，以德泽民，以公纳士，以正保身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274096_comment'></div>若乃势位极乎钧鼎，勋业溢乎旂常，此自所当有而未足道者也，不敢摭以为献云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1274096_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年12月</a>　是年冬，居兴国。十二月，兴国军学建成，王质作记。作品：《兴国军学记》<div id='poem_1274146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴国军学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274146")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274146'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274146'>学在郡之北，西附而东乡，旧者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274146_comment'></div>在郡之西，北附而南乡，新者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274146_comment'></div>其新者，今太守缙云叶公之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274146_comment'></div>请论昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274146_comment'></div>自绍兴二十年寖毁，历二十年大毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274146_comment'></div>奚以寖毁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274146_comment'></div>吏无政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274146_comment'></div>奚以大毁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274146_comment'></div>吏无志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274146_comment'></div>奚以弗新？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274146_comment'></div>吏无才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274146_comment'></div>请论今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274146_comment'></div>自乾道六年秋八月以兴，冬十二月以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274146_comment'></div>奚以必新？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274146_comment'></div>公有志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274146_comment'></div>奚以能新？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274146_comment'></div>公有才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274146_comment'></div>奚以能速？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274146_comment'></div>公有仁人长者之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274146_comment'></div>必新以志，能新以才，速亦才也，不以才，以仁人长者之心，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274146_comment'></div>请论志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274146_comment'></div>人各有私，异同相形，爱憎相搏，不挠者寡矣，而不挠者志健也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274146_comment'></div>请论才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274146_comment'></div>才各有量，抵其穷则咫尺不加进，毫毛不克举也，而不穷者才充也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274146_comment'></div>请论心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274146_comment'></div>夫民戚上而弗之欢敬，上而弗之爱，心不交也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274146_comment'></div>我与民为亲则劳佚同，民与我为亲则缓急同，蹶然动之，趯然其趋我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274146_comment'></div>此略也，请论详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274146_comment'></div>公始至，有事于先圣之庭，悼先圣之失其居，而惧己之弗虔其职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274146_comment'></div>公之言曰：「佛老之宫严且丽，率与皇居相侔，而先圣所庀乃弗及中下之庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274146_comment'></div>先圣吾天也，慢天者不祥，且吾所受制书学吾事也，违制者当论如律」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274146_comment'></div>于是公之志立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274146_comment'></div>既稽诸有司，则负上之逋以万计，负下之逋亦以万计，上以峻督，下以哀蕲，公之言曰：「峻不已则怒继之，哀不已则怨继之，上下交相愤也，志将何之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274146_comment'></div>于是公之志既立而未果行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274146_comment'></div>期年戢奸整慢，严藏啬出，而平时飞扬灭没之财并集，峻者夷，哀者怡矣，又推而应公上之羡征，满既往之宿负，待后来之急须，得衍算也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274146_comment'></div>于是公之志行也，此迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274146_comment'></div>请论理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274146_comment'></div>志者有意而无体，必有所依而行，才者所以为行志之具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274146_comment'></div>才者易纵而难收，微失所控则肆，故仁人长者之心所以为御才之器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274146_comment'></div>志健而才不足，则事弗济，才充而仁人长者之心弗笃，则事虽济而多伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274146_comment'></div>事且济而无伤，非三者相须而无亏，何以及此也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274146_comment'></div>此名也，请论实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274146_comment'></div>凡物，木章计，若竹若石若瓦若甓个计，灰石计，若铁若丹若垩斤计，取具为物，三十二万三千有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1274146_comment'></div>地为官者积弗取多，闲材不足则定其价而后市，赋其资而后输，视其愿则徇而从之，馀须皆如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1274146_comment'></div>凡工为庐事常廪，为土事常廪，有差不时，而抚其劳而扶其疾也，馀须又有差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1274146_comment'></div>既役，为工二万二千有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1274146_comment'></div>凡用以材事之质剂，命掌比之治者主之，凡掌比之治皆民之有力自重善持家耻犯法者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1274146_comment'></div>以役事之稍食，命掌学之政者主之，凡掌学之政皆士之秀且贤遵法度可踪迹者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1274146_comment'></div>民之良者劳于外，士之彦者持于内，奸者有以寓目而无以措手也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1274146_comment'></div>靡钱贯计五千一百有奇，粟石计九百三十有奇，无一而不至于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1274146_comment'></div>凡民受役要者咸喜，弗受役要者咸慕相劝而至不忍舍而归，此其情非有感乎利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1274146_comment'></div>凡室自殿若堂达于门，皆序而两之，自殿若堂衍于旁，皆挟而两之，暨他室楹计二百五十有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1274146_comment'></div>昔之所有必具而有加，其无也乃今有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1274146_comment'></div>此政也，请论人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1274146_comment'></div>公名模，字叔范，其考是为石林先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1274146_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1274146_comment'></div>可谓有子矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1274146_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年12月</a>　是年冬，居兴国。兴国军军营建成，王质作记。作品：《兴国四营记》<div id='poem_1274147' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274147' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274147?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴国四营记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274147")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274147_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274147'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274147'>兴国升军则有兵，自太平兴国二年始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274147_comment'></div>二十五之忠节，十五之效勇，十九之武雄、牢城，此凡军之额也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274147_comment'></div>其肄额自何年始也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274147_comment'></div>六百六十有七属诸禁，二百六十有七属诸厢，此凡军之籍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274147_comment'></div>其著籍自何年始也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274147_comment'></div>城之北少西，忠节、效勇、牢城营之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274147_comment'></div>城之东少北，武雄营之，此凡军之营也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274147_comment'></div>其建营自何年始也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274147_comment'></div>其废自建炎三年始也，其兴自乾道六年始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274147_comment'></div>六年则太守缙云叶公为政之再期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274147_comment'></div>六十有四以舍武雄，四十有九以舍忠节，三十以舍效勇，皆即其故营营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274147_comment'></div>又三十以舍牢城，更而西之，非其故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274147_comment'></div>四十四万二千一百有奇，积其物而计之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274147_comment'></div>六千九百六十有奇，积其庸而计之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274147_comment'></div>二千三百三十有奇，以贯计钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274147_comment'></div>二百八十有奇，以石计粟，市材召工之费也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274147_comment'></div>市者弗告亏，酬之优也，役者弗告劳，廪之厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274147_comment'></div>为坊五于其郭，为乡十有三、为里六十有五于其郊，无毫毛之自出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274147_comment'></div>于是兵之杂处者皆迁，兼其家者专舍之，止其身者合舍之，其身他隶而以其家自随者阙之，戍而未归者制其室数以待之，募而未集者分其地域饬其材事以待之，戍兵之归皆具，而未来者乃今有以逆之，则其为恩至衍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274147_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274147_comment'></div>月一其廪，岁两其缣，既有限也，征役则添，有给庆礼则横，有颁又弗常也，镌其有限弗常之禄而庐人之庐，甚矣其难也，且非惟其私而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274147_comment'></div>凡兵非涅不为兵，贵其辨于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274147_comment'></div>涅而去之，以某罪论，恶其无辨于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274147_comment'></div>不足，又以其服判之，其品七巾而至于屦，其采五白而至于绯，谓之军容，其弗遵者以某罪论，恶其无辨于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274147_comment'></div>不足又以其居别之，当舍而弗舍，弗当舍而舍，与弗当入而入，皆以某罪论，听而弗问，又以某罪论，甚恶其无辨于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274147_comment'></div>请有斗伤之禁，有博戏之禁，有禽犬之禁，有巫卜之禁，有饮禁，有滥禁，有逃禁，有盗禁，有诡名之禁，有匿奸之禁，有敛财之禁，有弛艺之禁，有窃造军器之禁，有私传兵式之禁，有出法物之禁，有结义社之禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274147_comment'></div>法也者驭兵之器也，营也者施法之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274147_comment'></div>官无寺无以施政也，士无学无以施业也，工无肆无以施事也，兵无营无以施法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274147_comment'></div>凡营别而谓之都，都有头总而谓之指挥，指挥有使，以伏事之仪制阶级之律，重则死之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274147_comment'></div>有兵于此，弗严则弗肃，弗肃是纵而菑之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274147_comment'></div>凡营有房，房有号，号有籍，损阙而失缮修，一日以某罪论，三日以某罪论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274147_comment'></div>若垣墉之败，则登时筑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274147_comment'></div>庇兵于此，弗整则弗安，弗安是锢而苦之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274147_comment'></div>登时较之，一日为多，一日较之，三日为多，四十三年而弗复，可以为多否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274147_comment'></div>岁秋八月乙丑，有令禁兵之占于籍者，以盈为度，其阙额钱毋输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274147_comment'></div>冬十一月乙酉，有令禁兵之疏于帐者，多阙弗登，必罚无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274147_comment'></div>此地旷而人稀，五方之游罕集，初皆以致兵为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274147_comment'></div>及是惮为兵者趯然动，疑为兵者毅然决，变其目之所习见而感其心之所乐为，则营之劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274147_comment'></div>奚为劝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274147_comment'></div>示其不恝然于彼，而覈其不漠然于此，此营之所以为劝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274147_comment'></div>官日以丑酉之令从事，孰敢不力，惟公之敏而功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274147_comment'></div>奚为敏而功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274147_comment'></div>无驱之以势而致之以道，此公之所以敏而功也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1274147_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d19293a0549e443780a86a5b7baedfc3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d19293a0549e443780a86a5b7baedfc3");'><span id='d19293a0549e443780a86a5b7baedfc3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1173')">1172-1173年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='d19293a0549e443780a86a5b7baedfc3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　是年回兴国，兴国守向澹将离任，宴请并有词相赠。作品：《临江仙（宴向守簇）》<div id='poem_73043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_73043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/73043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_73043")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_73043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_73043'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_73043'>千顷翠围遮绿净，菱花影落波中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_73043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_73043'>看看红锦漾清风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_73043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73043'>此时催入觐，烟浪拍云空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_73043_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73043'>伫见觚棱栖宝爵，旌旗全仗飞龙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_73043'>赭黄一点现真容。<div id='poem_sentence_4_73043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_73043'>御麻宣未毕，云镜上天东。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_73043_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　任枢密院编修官。其间曾回兴国，与于湖弟张孝忠（字王臣）会于兴国，嘱其辑于湖遗稿。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d1c761c57260405c85f307a7accf86da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d1c761c57260405c85f307a7accf86da");'><span id='d1c761c57260405c85f307a7accf86da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1189')">1175-1189年</a>，41-55岁</div><div id='d1c761c57260405c85f307a7accf86da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年2月</a>　二月，出通判荆南府，改吉州，皆不行，以主管成都府玉局观奉祠山居。作品：《退文序》<div id='poem_1274117' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>退文序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274117")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274117'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274117'>退文者，王子悔过之书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274117_comment'></div>王子少而为学问文章，年十有六而贡于里，二十有三而升于太学，二十有六而选于礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274117_comment'></div>其在太学也，得声为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274117_comment'></div>二十有七而朝野交称，辟召狎至，得声为尤多，实浅而声盈，于是以功名为可立就，而不知识未明，才未练，不足以当世故，而气已盛、志已高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274117_comment'></div>心之火为之宰，才之薪为之用，薪火相传益炎，而王子不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274117_comment'></div>岁辛巳一触祸，其可以知之矣，而弗知，曰：「人忌我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274117_comment'></div>岁丙戌再触祸，其可以知之矣，而又弗知，亦曰：「人嫉我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274117_comment'></div>岁辛卯三触祸，其可以知之矣，而又弗知，亦曰：「人弗容我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274117_comment'></div>岁乙未得罪，曰如是曰如是，乃始跃然悔，霍然悟，平生诸非参然毕陈于前，凛然惧，惨然悲，大变于顷刻之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274117_comment'></div>于是王子年四十有一而始造端为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274117_comment'></div>呜呼甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274117_comment'></div>吾心之躁也，悔躁则为静，吾心之轻也，悔轻则为重，吾心之急也，悔急则为缓，吾心之猛也，悔猛则为宽，吾心之侈也，悔侈则为俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274117_comment'></div>甚矣，吾心平生之多过而吾弗知也，然则奚以知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274117_comment'></div>曰：途弗穷则弗回，势弗极则弗变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274117_comment'></div>方其变故之未知也，吾心之火固自若也，增之益昌，殖之益滋，则吾之祸故可胜言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274117_comment'></div>及其变故之至也，如倾甘雨，如激大波，而吾心之火炽然者为萧然，则此变其可无也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274117_comment'></div>无此火弗能召此变，无此变弗能销此火，呜呼，此变其可无也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274117_comment'></div>有此变王子为君子，无此变王子为小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274117_comment'></div>非吾之资小人也，此火导而入之也，熏蒸燔灼之心既息，而温纯明净之心乃生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274117_comment'></div>向者，火所覆蔽而弗兴也，人以为得祸，曰：「一职之失也，三秩之镌也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274117_comment'></div>而吾以为得福，曰：「其失也有时而得，其镌也有时而复也，机缄所斡，锋铓所迫，廓然移风易俗于吾灵台之间，此不亦天下之至吉至祥也哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274117_comment'></div>且弗考其他，以吾身观之，形轻神怡志虑简，以吾家观之，上辑下睦门闾雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274117_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274117_comment'></div>吾心之火谢而弗为之主，吾之幽显咸安乐也，弗谓之吉祥可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274117_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274117_comment'></div>生于忧患，死于安乐，孟子决生死于忧患安乐之机而弗疑，吾乃今知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274117_comment'></div>得此变而后生，此变也者不至固不可，缓亦不可，不至蹈于死，缓则滨于死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274117_comment'></div>及是得之，能弗死而生，此天地之心，他人弗知，而吾于悔悟之际窥之审也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274117_comment'></div>今将何以持之，使坚曰畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274117_comment'></div>何以养之，使熟曰缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274117_comment'></div>作《六悔》，著其昔之非；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274117_comment'></div>作《六变》，著其今之是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274117_comment'></div>总而谓之《退书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274117_comment'></div>未悔则务进，既悔则务退，其相反盖理势然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274117_comment'></div>淳熙二年二月自序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1274117_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年11月27日</a>　十一月，有《跋苏给事放白鹇帖》<div id='poem_1274124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274124?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋苏给事放白鹇帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年11月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274124")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274124'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274124'>淳熙二年十一月二十七日早作，颍昌程君元鼎来谒，起立言曰：「昔先君巡检鼎之桃源，时给事苏公居提举使者幕府，以鼎为治，绍兴三十一年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274124_comment'></div>先君娶于柳氏展如之女，某之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274124_comment'></div>太师苏公之妹，展如之母也，于是与苏氏有连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274124_comment'></div>公资岩壑，喜鱼鸟之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274124_comment'></div>先君所部，山水深秀奇丽，黄石山者其尤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274124_comment'></div>其间得白鹇献之，护致者不谨伤焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274124_comment'></div>公绝欲愈之，不可得，怜而返诸先君，且属深纵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274124_comment'></div>乃即故处如公指，久之腾上高山颠，周视悲鸣，弗忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274124_comment'></div>又久之，一白鹇从他来，相与并立交呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274124_comment'></div>又久之，始皆徐飞去，岂其雌雄耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274124_comment'></div>仁心通乎异类，何其验之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274124_comment'></div>后数年先君尉光之固始以没，将终，季子在旁，戒曰：『我习言命，以金木水火土五者揆之，公他日必大，且其所存形诸白鹇者，可以推而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274124_comment'></div>天人之符较然，汝其识之』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274124_comment'></div>先君既丧，他书疏多遗散，独此帖不敢荒，先君之命囊别贮之，旦慕视惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274124_comment'></div>公今博大光明，为知名公卿，先君之言效矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274124_comment'></div>某将寿诸石，君其为我书之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274124_comment'></div>余曰：「说如是，帖安在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274124_comment'></div>程君发诸袖中，余掇视之，慨然太息曰：「仁者人也，合而言之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274124_comment'></div>盖其大与天地同量，而其端以恻隐之心充之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274124_comment'></div>孟子之言，天下学士所信，舍牛可以致王，救孺子可以保四海，其仁至不可胜用者，自无欲害人始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274124_comment'></div>子先君以白鹇验苏公，此有道者之鉴也，而余将何以赞之，子休矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274124_comment'></div>自白鹇充之，可使斯世为尧舜成康，此孟子之论，而非余创建者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274124_comment'></div>子毋疑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274124_comment'></div>公今为徽猷阁待制，镇当涂，太师文忠公之曾孙，其学力盖真能扩充者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274124_comment'></div>名昭广，字邦振，盖程君所道其先君者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274124_comment'></div>今附见之，来者得以知焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1274124_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　是年居兴国。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年2月</a>　居兴国。二月，大冶县学建成，为作记。作品：《兴国军大冶县学记》<div id='poem_1274152' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274152' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274152?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴国军大冶县学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274152")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274152_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274152'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274152'>天子非人才无与共治天下，人才也者，其源在乡，其流在郡，其归在朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274152_comment'></div>积石河之源也，岷山江之源也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274152_comment'></div>播而九之，河之流也，别而九之，又三江之流也，其归则同入于海也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274152_comment'></div>河且南且东，至于华阴、底柱、孟津、大伾，过大陆而北之，此而见河之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274152_comment'></div>江所历曰沱，曰澧，曰东陵，曰汇，曰中江，皆东趋，此而见江之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274152_comment'></div>皆未逾海之为归，其泽溥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274152_comment'></div>人才在乡不若在郡国，在郡国不若在朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274152_comment'></div>朝廷人才之海也，而其源则浚于其乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274152_comment'></div>周制，士有秀，自乡而升之司徒，则以选士名之，拔于其群也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274152_comment'></div>选士又有秀，自司徒而升之学，则以俊士名之，尤于其选也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274152_comment'></div>既升则弗征，则以造士名之，与民别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274152_comment'></div>造士又有秀，大乐正以告于王而升诸司马，则以进士名之，与士别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274152_comment'></div>进士又有贤，司马以告于王而官之、爵之、禄之，此人才之滥觞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274152_comment'></div>周官三百六十，总以六卿，内外高下而别之，乃克用人，盖人才皆繇此出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274152_comment'></div>今之天下为里若干而属诸乡，为乡若干而属诸县，县也者乡之会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274152_comment'></div>此论士之积石、岷山，导之则九国被其惠，否则万物壅其泽，其利害顾不大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274152_comment'></div>公来为是邑，则曰财匮当理，讼滞当决，有司事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274152_comment'></div>学校弗振，则人才弗茂，人才弗茂，则国奚须、君奚赖哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274152_comment'></div>国事也，君事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274152_comment'></div>古者三十年为一世，州以士献郡，弗以名闻，阅世而且过之，其才小不展于州县，大不施于朝廷，士奚怍，有司之惭可既乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274152_comment'></div>何为咎有司也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274152_comment'></div>县令于民有父母之道也，于士有师之道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274152_comment'></div>民弗兴，咎在父母，士弗作，咎在师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274152_comment'></div>公甚病之，则以告凡邑之民曰：「学也者为国养才，非虚拘夫士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274152_comment'></div>士也者为国养德，非空廪夫官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274152_comment'></div>德足矣，位及之，所以训治汝等既富且良，而为美俗也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274152_comment'></div>于是役兴而民欢趋，则又以告凡邑之士曰：「学也者非徒其文也，学之本在道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274152_comment'></div>士也者非徒其貌也，士之实在心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274152_comment'></div>所以推之，治国平天下，惟公所学是资也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274152_comment'></div>于是工休而士竞劝，则以请东平王某书之，公不自有，又以告凡邑之士若民曰：「学也者天子制之，有司行之，当戴天子，无思有司，《诗》不云乎『周王寿考，遐不作人』，知本也夫」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274152_comment'></div>于是以时释菜于先圣之庭，再拜稽首，咏歌君师之德，以为天而后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274152_comment'></div>某为之述曰：丙申冬十一月二十八日绪功也，丁酉春二月十五日讫事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274152_comment'></div>三十有七者其楹也，西而北者其方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274152_comment'></div>其来请者，周君之奇、朱君绂、何君若、董君维新、万君钧、陈君勋，学之儒生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274152_comment'></div>其更新者，潘公子韶，邑之令君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274152_comment'></div>公三山人，贤而有政事文章，观此其他不问而可知也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1274152_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　是年居兴国。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　居兴国，有《平政堂记》<div id='poem_1274154' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274154' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274154?labeling=true' target='_blank'>平政堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274154")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274154_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274154'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274154'>上即位之十七年，诏以某人为兴国太守，凡亲若故咸止君勿往，曰：「究之习兴国者，濒湖为郭，其民与龟鱼蘋瓜杂居，水归则葭苇莽苍，又与狐兔相参也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274154_comment'></div>是岁诸大吏绳是邦以法者若干，诸小民诉是邦以牒者若干，诸吏若胥大若小重若轻论者若干，诸当输不输钱若干、粟若干，诸当办不办兵若干，甲若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274154_comment'></div>推此类具言之又若干，其何以当之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274154_comment'></div>君曰：「君命也，将若之何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274154_comment'></div>既至信然，某人欲引去，某人欲引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274154_comment'></div>或趋君勿留，曰：「兴国久不可为也，而今为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274154_comment'></div>凡仓庾若府库存者若干，弗存者若干，凡文符可报者若干，不可报者若干，凡城郭若乡里可督者若干，不可督者若干，他不堪谁何者又若干，其何以承之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274154_comment'></div>君曰：「君事也，又将若之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274154_comment'></div>古之为吏者以职守为业，以官守为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274154_comment'></div>汉制间即所居之官为姓号传子孙，而疾病休谒汤沐则归而与其家相见，其勤且专者虽汤沐亦弗出，犹有纯世之遗风焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274154_comment'></div>古者重于以身臣人，由此之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274154_comment'></div>今士大夫之家固有不幸而当其败坏者，则亦极力所致而已，未有弃而他之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274154_comment'></div>使为吏者举择夫便利美好居之，则远外之人谁与共理者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274154_comment'></div>上不鄙为弗能，而俾之当此门、持此家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274154_comment'></div>人主以天下为家者也，众建官师，分职内外，无非干蛊之子承德而用誉斯为亨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274154_comment'></div>二爻干母，三爻干父，而终爻则父母之蛊皆弗及焉，故曰『不事王侯，高尚其事』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274154_comment'></div>此季夏园公之伦，非委质事人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274154_comment'></div>且我方其未来则固徐氏之主也，今委此身任此邦，徐氏则传舍路人，而兴国则家也，观夫徐氏滋轻矣，其敢不力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274154_comment'></div>若履危涉难，与死生相轇轕，在劳心平时且吉壤者不可同年语也，其又将奚辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274154_comment'></div>有所难于此则有所难于彼，慎重可以为事君之大义，非耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274154_comment'></div>已而反侧者绥之使安，离散者敛之使集，愁劳者保之使康，迫蹙者弛之使宽，而后废玩者震之使耸，豪梗者钤之使戢，逋滞者整之使齐，彫敝者厉之使精，宽猛相济，刚柔适时，而兴国之政乃平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274154_comment'></div>凡邦国官府之财赋、凡官吏卒伍之稍食、凡祭祀宾客之劳礼、凡都鄙稍甸之政令，无或过，无或不及，而兴国之政大平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274154_comment'></div>惟其阅义理明，阅世故熟，致此非难也，而不择剧易，不间美恶，以大公至正克其心，汲黯难于淮阳而君易于兴国，视古人有加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274154_comment'></div>其堂凡辨地域，凡审面势，凡赋功绪，凡饬财用事，皆弗著，著其大略而系之辞，从民志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274154_comment'></div>辞曰：峨峨其巅，穹翠摩天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274154_comment'></div>君登斯堂，意不在山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274154_comment'></div>皎皎其沚，江湖表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274154_comment'></div>君登斯堂，意不在水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274154_comment'></div>安在其心，在帝之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274154_comment'></div>有露有霜，有秋有春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274154_comment'></div>维帝克圣，维民是徇，不刚不柔，大公至正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274154_comment'></div>维君体之，又率履之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274154_comment'></div>君明臣良，相协济之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274154_comment'></div>有熙斯辰，有偃斯虹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274154_comment'></div>万声一欢，往来憧憧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274154_comment'></div>有晏斯居，昼律夜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274154_comment'></div>弗猜弗惊，浮龟沈鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274154_comment'></div>君之归矣，民之思矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274154_comment'></div>有茇其阴，无斁遗矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1274154_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　丞相赵雄请其出山，而以“事老父”婉辞。作品：《与赵丞相书》<div id='poem_1274098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与赵丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274098")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274098'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274098'>某伏以季春正时，恭惟咸有一德，克享天心，如伊尹之暨成汤，佑我烈祖，格于皇天，如傅说之迪高宗，明灵降佑，亿兆知归，钧候起居万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274098_comment'></div>某伏读十一月八日制书，咨禹之辞亮采，惠畴之训甚切，命毕之辞正色，率下之谟甚勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274098_comment'></div>某所知者神州之境将复，上道之日将行，其关诸度数，协诸阴阳，天之所为不可得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274098_comment'></div>虽管窥蠡测，窃知其土苴绪馀，亦不能言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274098_comment'></div>非独管蠡不能言，虽仪、秦之辩，深析万宇之情，亦不能言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274098_comment'></div>虽庄、列之机，普观六合之表，亦不能言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274098_comment'></div>虽佛祖之慧，洞照万劫之初，亦不能言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274098_comment'></div>德山禅师有云：「穷诸玄辨，若一毫致于太虚，竭世枢机，似一滴投于巨壑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274098_comment'></div>考之吾儒，所谓太仓之稊米，大泽之礧空，此某所以不敢重缄叠幅，致赞咏揄扬之辞，自知其绘画之无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274098_comment'></div>然有一言敢述万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274098_comment'></div>自艺祖以来，与国同姓而登庸，举其尤彰明较著者凡三人焉：运属建隆时，则有忠献赵公，削平九牧，混一万殊，有宋之业开创灵长者由此之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274098_comment'></div>运属绍兴，时则有忠简赵公，扶颠持危，拨乱反正，有宋之业复兴再昌者由此之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274098_comment'></div>运属淳熙，时则有我公，有忠献公削平应变之略而守天下之大经，有忠简公元镇持正之操而达天下之大权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274098_comment'></div>有斯人，生斯世，遇斯时，宅斯地，此孟子所谓兴王名世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274098_comment'></div>以其数则过矣，以其时考之则可矣，其可谓非天乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274098_comment'></div>其可谓非天乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274098_comment'></div>窃独未知相公经纬错综四海九州之度，固已指掌于前，孰为先，孰为后，孰为缓，孰为急，孰为第一议，孰为第二议，熟为推毂，孰为合尖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274098_comment'></div>相公必有以处之矣，而某未之或知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274098_comment'></div>兹事姑止，某有至危至迫至哀至穷之情，敢冀相公试垂听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274098_comment'></div>相公应期乘运，实在己酉，而老父生于庚寅，某生于乙卯，揆之常情，事相公之日甚长，事老父之日差短，兴念及此，莫知身世之所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274098_comment'></div>迫世垂年，仕于遐邑，欲挽而留之，少安温凊之养，而老父之宦情未衰，欲胜而上之，稍进优清之位，而某之力不足，将若之何，将若之何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274098_comment'></div>昔丞相仙井虞公盖尝造化老父以湖北之帅属，又尝造化老父以江南之帅属，非独以不肖子而埏埴老父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274098_comment'></div>虞公笃孝于老太师，某尝为之画赞，有云「五桂芬芬，流香如水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274098_comment'></div>今茂其一，尚馀其四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274098_comment'></div>三槐森森，成阴满庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274098_comment'></div>其一属子，其二及孙」，大略云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274098_comment'></div>不独兴公之击节，又动公之伤神，所以某之肺肝及于老父之间，而公不忍拒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274098_comment'></div>伏观先太师克襄大事之时，相公不鄙，状其行赐之，俾制挽章为灵輀之先驱，相公尚亦记之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274098_comment'></div>其词盖云：「叩阍凛凛疏三通，归社萧萧酒一钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274098_comment'></div>龙卧南阳呼不醒，鹏飞北海去无踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274098_comment'></div>无年及见安车召，有子能荒大国封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274098_comment'></div>想见功名心未死，亦随江汉去朝宗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274098_comment'></div>其辞虽陋而已有验矣，可谓先见乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274098_comment'></div>今老太师端居上清，俯视尘寰，未必慨然于功名之语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274098_comment'></div>某辄敢凭此良缘，仰于洪造，相公其动念于老父耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274098_comment'></div>其不动念于老父耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274098_comment'></div>虞公之旧恩可援以为例耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274098_comment'></div>不可援以为例耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274098_comment'></div>皆惟相公之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274098_comment'></div>锡类之仁，圣贤之盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274098_comment'></div>方相公期运未至，从容于红莲绿水之时，彼此为之嬉笑者弥日，今某可谓困矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274098_comment'></div>呜呼，使之困者天也，使之不困者相公也，相公亦天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274098_comment'></div>王仲淹云：「使如晦而得志于万民，其犹天乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1274098_comment'></div>天下皆戴相公之天，而某戴之尤深，天未尝有私覆也，某之情私也，人之所欲天必从之，天未尝拒私情也，顾其情如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1274098_comment'></div>盖有似私而实公者，某之所陈，老父之辞是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1274098_comment'></div>相公哀之，相公怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1274098_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1274098_comment'></div>仙凡之路异，云泥之分殊，可以目睹而不可以迹亲，可以声彻而不可以足至，惟相公厚护栋梁，永毗箕翼，伟绩塞乎鼎彝，茂勋溢乎旂常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1274098_comment'></div>某未毕馀生，尚庶几见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1274098_comment'></div>无以报效相公者，独公之所不能形容，某能发而为文，著而成章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1274098_comment'></div>徂徕庆历之诗所谓「维仲淹弼，一夔一契」，壮哉，崇二老之炜煜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1274098_comment'></div>某则不然，近取诸身则有「赓歌」之元首股肱，远取诸物则有《乾》之风虎云龙，参天两地而倚数，则有禹、皋陶五百岁之运，幽赞于神明而生蓍，则有傅说、吕望梦卜之祥，庶合于圣人之遗意而为不负于相公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1274098_comment'></div>徂徕复生，傥以为然乎，相公裁之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1274098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　是年，有诗。作品：《赠黄君》<div id='poem_548736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠黄君</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548736")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548736'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548736'>君见雪山谭晦庵，晦庵南北隔山川。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548736'>有命归来如二老，不然隐去自三贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548736'>晦庵今年登五十，鬓华未改目光力。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548736'>徘徊吴楚已多年，晦庵不急苍生急。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548736'>君行车马衣冠衢，亦有晦庵相似无。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548736'>君臣庆会第一格，晦庵何日何时须。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548736'>横渠虽没尚可作，平生此事喜商略。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548736'>君当长跪问横渠，子细平章句教错。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548736'>大江朔风多涌波，上江下江且婆娑。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548736'>古时贤士一时有，奈此庚辛甲乙何<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548736'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_548736_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_548736'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_548736_0'>⑴ 自注：黄君来过，谈士大夫甲乙及晦庵为详。所从之游者如此，不凡可卜也。君于（原作子，据孔本、秦本改）通老端明为族孙，故有士子风格云。　原案：朱子年谱生于建炎庚戌，此诗当是淳熙六年己亥所作。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_548736_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年12月20日</a>　十二月二十日，知兴国军徐行简放罢，有词送别。作品：《临江仙（和徐守圣可）》<div id='poem_73043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_73043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/73043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临江仙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_73043")'>王质</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_73043'>千顷翠围遮绿净，菱花影落波中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_73043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_73043'>看看红锦漾清风。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　居兴国，与陆游唱和。作品：《寄题陆务观渔隐》<div id='poem_548737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548737?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题陆务观渔隐<span class='inlineComment2'>（原案：此诗当是淳熙七年所作。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548737")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548737_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548737'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548737'>渔隐渔隐在何方，海门潮白江沙黄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548737'>吾尝袖手江之旁，西兴草树烟苍苍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548737'>欲往从之道阻长，波涛澎湃不敢航。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548737'>仰观河汉翔鹔鹴，安得与之俱颉颃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548737'>得非兰亭会诸王，清湍茂竹联崇冈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548737'>无乃镜湖留知章，兰蘅风露生寒凉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548737'>不然此地何铿锵，宿昔名胜沈光芒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548737'>俟今焜耀名方昌，恨不登时到侯乡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548737'>循墙三匝徐升堂，观山观水观松篁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548737'>以及鱼鸟同徜徉，而俟南益仍西凉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_548737'>鸿雁同天不同行，爱而不见魂飞扬。<div id='poem_sentence_11_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_548737'>梦从县圃周扶桑，逢迎跪揖如平常。<div id='poem_sentence_12_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_548737'>齿牙砰磕摇风霜，秦汉魏晋周隋唐。<div id='poem_sentence_13_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_548737'>江河滚滚倾兴亡，指画所隐声琅琅。<div id='poem_sentence_14_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_548737'>欢喜奇特不可当，继以惊愕怀慞惶。<div id='poem_sentence_15_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_548737'>倏忽烟雾轻腾骧，径跨越峤超吴泷。<div id='poem_sentence_16_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_548737'>杉烟竹月无时荒，白蒲青荇春悠扬。<div id='poem_sentence_20_548737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　与知兴国军张釜唱和，有诗。作品：《题张君量恩波寺》<div id='poem_548843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>荷柳松竹赠答<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>仆赠荷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548703")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548703_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_548703_0'>① 原案：此诗当是孝宗淳熙八年所作。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548703'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548703'>仆赠荷，吾友清阴多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548703_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548704?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>荷逊柳</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548704'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548704'>荷逊柳，短茁非脩茎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548704'>焉如子妙密，腾起敷层阴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548704_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548704'>明月上，子勿障，主欲务遐观，清宇任昭旷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_548704_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548705?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>柳逊竹</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548705'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548705'>柳逊竹，弱植短奇节。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548705'>戛玉仍铿金，难攀子清绝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548705_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548705'>主睡酣，毋惊醒，迟主江湖归，相与献清影。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_548705_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548706?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>竹逊松</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548706'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548706'>竹逊松，古气摩空缠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548706'>铁石作风骨，可以班主贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548706'>虚空中，走河海，主不好世音，子盍宏天籁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_548706_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548707?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>松答仆</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548707'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548707'>松答仆，奉主愿尽心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548707'>护以虬龙威，娱以金玉音。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548707'>作炎夏，作凛秋，愿主爱玉体，五夜增轻裘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_548707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　是年居兴国。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　居兴国，正月，《绍陶录》撰成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年6月</a>　居兴国，六月，为祈雨而作有《三圣坛龙祠记》<div id='poem_1274155' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274155' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274155?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三圣坛龙祠记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274155")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274155_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274155'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274155'>淳熙十有一年六月，雨不以时至，太守池阳王公曰：「先成民而后致力于神，古之训也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274155_comment'></div>凡治具考古之度，相今之宜，以次毕讲，乃有事于上帝，又有事于群龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274155_comment'></div>公曰：「在田在渊，且在天龙之所止，行也，宜求夫并野并水而扬灵，即其所止飨之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274155_comment'></div>东隔堤起阜，屹立平湖之中，势不甚高而巨浸莫能踰，相传与水俱升，盖神之久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274155_comment'></div>公曰：「龙实震为之，雷亦震为之，正东之卦也，是地当用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274155_comment'></div>吏以祠龙之旧仪进，公曰：「祖宗宪章，至天圣迄嘉祐愈粹，今皇祐之成式在，是法当用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274155_comment'></div>公又曰：「是礼也文，其何以将之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274155_comment'></div>《中庸》不云乎『至诚不息』，不息则久，久则悠远，悠远则博厚，博厚则高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274155_comment'></div>博厚配地，高明配天，悠久无疆，天地以诚而交参，神其舍诸」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274155_comment'></div>公又曰：「是理也隐，其何以表之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274155_comment'></div>《中庸》不云乎：「视之而弗见，听之而弗闻，体物而不可遗，使天下之人齐明盛服以承祭祀，洋洋乎如在其上，如在其左右」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274155_comment'></div>夫微之显，诚之不可掩如此，夫诚可会幽明为一家，神其彰矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274155_comment'></div>闻者信居半，疑居半，咸曰：「圣人之言在世，何其取用者多而收功者鲜也，今将于公乎验之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274155_comment'></div>丁亥礼行，是日阴云生，戊子礼成，是日膏泽洽，越三四日至足而有馀，越七八日荐至而不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274155_comment'></div>于是疑者皆信，信者皆坚，然后知神道非邈，圣言非诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274155_comment'></div>某以为公致天泽厚民生，其功小，使夫圣人之言信于天下之心，其功大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274155_comment'></div>天下不取信于圣人，圣人不见信于天下，虽有粟，安得而食诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274155_comment'></div>公名某，字某，其学导源于鲁而会流于邹，故言行之气象蔼如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274155_comment'></div>信是理深，相是礼笃，起是工敏，求是文切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274155_comment'></div>汴都赵某以之观是举审，纪是迹实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274155_comment'></div>汶阳王某以之建诸天地而不悖，质诸鬼神而无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274155_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274155_comment'></div>此文之所以为作也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1274155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年7月</a>　居兴国，七月，因得罪永兴知县赵伯彬而降一官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年8月</a>　致书周必大。作品：《与周枢密益公书》<div id='poem_1274099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274099?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周枢密益公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274099")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274099'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274099'>某伏以季春之月在天为中和之候，在世为清明之辰，于《易》应《泰》，于《诗》应《颂》，于《书》应《典》，而大贤皆乘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274099_comment'></div>钧候起居万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274099_comment'></div>某戴天不知天之恩，惟知其一，曰「予我以善」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274099_comment'></div>根戴相公亦不知相公之恩，惟知其一，曰「举我以言语妙天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274099_comment'></div>盖十有三年之前，相府宾次骤见而骤语，五字才出，一语才已，而雍公已降阶，相公已升堂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274099_comment'></div>古人以不见授意，儒门有之，荷筱丈人之类是也，他门亦多有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274099_comment'></div>以一字两字授意，儒门有之，曾参之答「唯」，孟懿子之得「无违」之类是也，他门亦多有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274099_comment'></div>立见一而揖三，立语一而字五，虽甚遽，已亦足矣，而某犹不知所谓，则是土木也，则是蛙蚓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274099_comment'></div>岁月朝推暮移，而此五字不推不移，形骸日迁月化，而此五字不迁不化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274099_comment'></div>然某窃有不安者，近时可谓于斯为盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274099_comment'></div>言语俊而庄，则有薛公叔云，此一妙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274099_comment'></div>言语秀而丽，则有李公粹伯，此一妙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274099_comment'></div>言语淡而雅，则有吕公伯恭，此一妙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274099_comment'></div>言语严而健，则有尹公少稷，此一妙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274099_comment'></div>言语约而肃，则有刘公文潜，此一妙也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274099_comment'></div>言语粹而明，则有洪公景卢，此一妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274099_comment'></div>大概如此，可略举不可尽述也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274099_comment'></div>某何人斯，言语之妙已不足以当之，惟有数种各具一妙，自惟妙天下者此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274099_comment'></div>敢惟相公陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274099_comment'></div>某病僻，平生不能曲随簧鼓以唇吻为公论，旁联钩锁以党援为良朋，以为男子不能自立门庭，而依人藩篱，不能自守魂魄，而附野草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274099_comment'></div>每见古人特立独行，不为路人移转脚根者，明目张胆慕之，故人以某为好异，此一病甚大，而自以为妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274099_comment'></div>某又有痴病，平生嗜古过于嗜刍豢，好书甚于好颜色，才遇得意，忘饥忘渴，而身世兼忘，或经月，或经年，亦有经月经年不事此者，故人以某为无常，此一病甚大，而自以为妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274099_comment'></div>某又有狂病，平生耽江山，悦林泉，有意无传，则寄夫山水之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274099_comment'></div>常绕湖百匝，自卷雪至灵仙，一夕而成百咏，尝榜江千里，自兴国至池阳，顺流而不知，故人以某为抱恙，此一病甚大，而自以为妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274099_comment'></div>某又有懒病，平时闭门却扫，佛来不著，祖来推出，虽未为息交绝游，然宾朋亦稀，轮鞅亦寡，书疏不能为苛谨，礼重必简，情真必切，如是而已，故人以某为轻物，此一病甚大，而自以为妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274099_comment'></div>又有拗病，有蠢病，不可胜言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274099_comment'></div>啖土炭为珍羞，岂非受疾之奇哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274099_comment'></div>今幻妙皆除，惟相公所言真妙者始绪正而卒成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274099_comment'></div>且如谈诗自知音始，世之知音者少而古声不复传于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274099_comment'></div>隋、唐之际，河汾之区犹歌某诗和某诗，而宣、政之间乡人窦氏尚间能以诗入律，则其废亦未甚云久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274099_comment'></div>既不可复考，姑且正音、正训、正章、正句、正字、正物、正用、正迹、正事、正人而为十正，吴公才老得其一节，而不得其大方，要可以推其他矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274099_comment'></div>少使讹舛稍归于次第，而后因情求意，皆吾心腹肺肠之事，此某欲妙而未能妙者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274099_comment'></div>又如谈《易》自知数始，世之知数者少，惟康节以此遗后人，为入《易》之门，而人多因辞生理，惟其意之所欲，不知圣人一字不虚发，寓理于数，寓数于理，旁通曲贯，数理并行，所谓吉凶悔咎皆有自而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274099_comment'></div>故以邵意、邵辞、邵数、邵理、邵诀、邵验而为六邵，稍见康节之绪馀而不为艰深，尽属平易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274099_comment'></div>非如张公文饶之有所泥而不导当世以通津，此某欲妙而未能妙者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274099_comment'></div>兹事且置，过此以往，时和岁丰，使米贱帛低，上恩流及于下，民得以销日度年，此燮理之妙，有望于相公者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274099_comment'></div>盗销贼宁，官不为贪，吏不为酷，金木稀，文符简，而安静于田闾，此康济之妙，有望于相公者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274099_comment'></div>王子渊贤臣之妙，陵士衡功臣之妙，吕化光勋臣之妙，至于韩退之元和一表妙之又妙，石守道庆历一范一富之颂妙之更妙，必有任此者，而某未之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274099_comment'></div>既老且衰，卒有不胜洒扫之职，不得谢一语之恩于数仞之下，生有馀辜，死有遗恨，是以言此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274099_comment'></div>某惶恐惶恐，死罪死罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1274099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　居兴国，晚年撰成研究《诗经》的著作《诗总闻》二十卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1188')">1187-1188年</a>　是年居兴国。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年1月19日</a>　正月，在兴国去世。葬兴国永兴县牛头山。<br /></div>
-----end

杭州

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1158')">1157-1158年</a>，23-24岁</div><div id='fd09ed3eebfe43f28f47104cb9cb45f7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　入太学，从张孝祥游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　与户部侍郎荣薿有交。有诗。作品：《西斋落成呈荣茂世》<div id='poem_548822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
