id='poem_sentence_20_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_548893'>输怀情缱绻，接语步竛竮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑺</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_21_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_548893'>岩壑多空帐，江湖少带笭。<div id='poem_sentence_22_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_548893'>姚崇资倜傥，葛亮意丁宁。<div id='poem_sentence_23_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_548893'>秀气横连霍，洪恩沇溢荥。<div id='poem_sentence_24_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_548893'>德威驯虎兕，道力化蝗螟。<div id='poem_sentence_25_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_548893'>烽燧寒边堠，桑麻蔽远坰。<div id='poem_sentence_26_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_548893'>农熙牛𧥄𧥄，兵劲马駉駉。<div id='poem_sentence_27_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_548893'>雁泽宽心驻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑻</sup>，龙沙侧耳听<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑼</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_28_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_548893'>檄囊停插羽，纶阁缓摇铃。<div id='poem_sentence_29_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_548893'>周廪仍多黍，尧阶再产蓂。<div id='poem_sentence_30_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_548893'>长杨荒御宿，茂草鞠虚囹。<div id='poem_sentence_31_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_548893'>忽化双林火，俄流五丈星。<div id='poem_sentence_32_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_548893'>更生游佛国<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑽</sup>，中卫立仙庭。<div id='poem_sentence_33_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_548893'>陵寝稽朝洛，王师寖度泾。<div id='poem_sentence_34_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_548893'>萧何虽镇蜀，韩信未踰陉。<div id='poem_sentence_35_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_548893'>鹤踞新华表，鲸归旧紫溟。<div id='poem_sentence_36_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_548893'>月明空皎皎，风远但泠泠。<div id='poem_sentence_37_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_548893'>蚤岁蒙推奖，多时备使令。<div id='poem_sentence_38_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_548893'>盘餐传舴艋<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑾</sup>，茵吐溅篁箳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑿</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_39_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_548893'>追琢参群玉，调和作五鲭<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：公不鄙，数以清贯处之。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_40_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_548893'>自从悲殄瘁，谁弗念伶俜。<div id='poem_sentence_41_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_548893'>道路纡脩阻，音尘堕杳冥。<div id='poem_sentence_42_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_548893'>口呿惟墨墨，头点自惺惺。<div id='poem_sentence_43_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_548893'>发白心随老，灯青目不瞑。<div id='poem_sentence_44_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_548893'>有声号井络，无路挽车軨。<div id='poem_sentence_45_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_548893'>睿意思元老，徽章播大廷。<div id='poem_sentence_46_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_548893'>云台先邓禹，烟阁重房龄。<div id='poem_sentence_47_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_548893'>未解联温赞，何劳勒固铭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒀</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_48_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_548893'>孙多骐骥骨，子悉凤凰翎<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：公之子学问道法皆茂。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_49_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_548893'>生死虽无憾，哀荣不忍聆。<div id='poem_sentence_50_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_548893'>一从云隔汉，两见水漫汀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⒁</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_51_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_548893'>飞梦风翻絮，浮生浪捲萍。<div id='poem_sentence_52_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_548893'>西尘黯沈日，双照泪荧荧<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：兴国视蜀门为西。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_53_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_548893'></div><div id='poem_sentence_54_548893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_548893'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_548893_0'>⑴ 自注：公时为参谋，勒兵督战，却之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_548893_0'>⑵ 自注：有画采石战图鬻之者，公俨立山巅，旁标曰“虞舍人”。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_548893_0'>⑶ 自注：公罢政，甫至仙井，即趣召。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_548893_0'>⑷ 自注：公为江淮、荆、襄、川、陕参谋、制置、宣谕、宣抚，凡五出使。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_548893_0'>⑸ 自注：公为周签书、同知、知院及使，参政左右，皆遍历。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_548893_0'>⑹ 自注：公当国，推挽贤才甚众，今所用多其宾客也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_548893_0'>⑺ 自注：公当国，接人务尽其情，或至跛踦，而公不倦也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_28_548893_0'>⑻ 自注：西北来归之民数万口，赖公以安。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_28_548893_0'>⑼ 自注：敌中闻公姓名，辄变色，令谍者潜摹公像以归观之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_33_548893_0'>⑽ 自注：有人入冥，见先太师为更生佛。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_39_548893_0'>⑾ 自注：公航江入蜀视师，乘小艇，公舟时传嘉餐馈之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_39_548893_0'>⑿ 自注：尝元宵侍宴醉吐，公探囊发药饵之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_48_548893_0'>⒀ 自注：公以文章见期，然未有以报也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_51_548893_0'>⒁ 自注：别公二年而公薨。得公书，前未薨十日手泽也。其略云：景文之身可以升沈，而文章不与时高下。哀哉！</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_548893_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年2月</a>　二月，虞允文薨，有祭文哀悼。作品：《祭虞丞相文》<div id='poem_1274185' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274185' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274185?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭虞丞相文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274185")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274185_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274185'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274185'>采石之危，危于淝水，淝距长江，尚隔千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274185_comment'></div>岐亮之锐，锐于苻坚，秉帜登坛，刑马告天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274185_comment'></div>维公之功，功于安石，彼乃处中，公切凭敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274185_comment'></div>采石之急，急于澶渊，澶当其冲，敌顿莫前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274185_comment'></div>岐亮之才，才于宗真，华夷悉俱，百万是群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274185_comment'></div>维公之难，难于莱国，潜、超犹全，锜、权皆北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274185_comment'></div>自古强敌，三寇江淮，瓜步徐归，国无人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274185_comment'></div>焘至平城，命歼宗爱，厥躯虽夷，厥师弗败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274185_comment'></div>惟坚与亮，宗覆身殒，天耶人耶，鉴此其警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274185_comment'></div>坚还长安，馀年而毙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274185_comment'></div>亮殂维扬，期月而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274185_comment'></div>靖康、建炎，嗟公生迟，早三十年，强敌奚为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274185_comment'></div>国有丕烈，天与英杰，钓渭筑岩，如印钥符节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274185_comment'></div>将定淮蔡，遗元和度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274185_comment'></div>将复河湟，遗会昌德裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274185_comment'></div>克西雍东洛，至德维郭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274185_comment'></div>下两淮三关，显德维朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274185_comment'></div>在辛巳绍兴，岂天无心，弗有斯厄，弗有斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274185_comment'></div>维宋无极，维功无斁，乘云空飞，矫首何及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274185_comment'></div>貌在凌烟，功在太常，名在四方，以暨八荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274185_comment'></div>哀摧我肝，液涨我睫，欲报无从，一念千劫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1274185_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年4月</a>　四月，作《濠州双穗堂记》<div id='poem_1274151' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274151' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274151?labeling=true' target='_blank'>濠州双穗堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274151")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274151_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274151'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274151'>淳熙元年夏四月，得麦于濠梁之郊，一本而二岐，太守张公曰：「『桑无附枝，麦秀两岐』，此吾祖渔阳之诵也，吾何以得之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274151_comment'></div>凡州之人咸曰：「维时穰哉，维民康哉，太守良哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274151_comment'></div>公曰：「异亩同颖之禾，唐叔得之献诸天子，天子得之归诸周公，『归禾』之书是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274151_comment'></div>周公得之旅天子之命，作《嘉禾》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274151_comment'></div>成王不肯有，叔父是归，周公犹曰天子之命也敢辞，况唐叔哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274151_comment'></div>国有祥，天子承之，其不有谦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274151_comment'></div>臣扬之，罔敢居之，在小臣尤宜也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274151_comment'></div>凡州之人又曰：「往者资政沈公使淮西，其未入为大臣也，有芝开其先焉，堂以识之，其名为玉芝者也，于是濡须重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274151_comment'></div>公诚不自有，毋亦肯堂以宠吾邦」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274151_comment'></div>公谢不敢，曰：「小儗大，非伦也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274151_comment'></div>凡州之人又曰：「五谷奚别，而麦见谓首种，其有以也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274151_comment'></div>天将兴周，以来麰贻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274151_comment'></div>及其降也，《春秋》他谷不书，至麦禾不成则书之，非末矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274151_comment'></div>斯堂也者，重民事，承天休，太守之职也，公其毋忽」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274151_comment'></div>公又谢不敢，弗能得，则左其治之偏而堂之，公曰：「以双穗名，若何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274151_comment'></div>凡州之人曰：「宜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274151_comment'></div>公曰：「宜则当书」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274151_comment'></div>来告曰：「茍宜书，公其为我书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274151_comment'></div>渔阳在汉为宛人，我于今为安丰人，间因乱避地而去之，残牒尚有考焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274151_comment'></div>今逆数渔阳为建武初元，得一千二百馀年，而是物也复出，大惧无以绍前人之休，然天子之泽，非我之力也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274151_comment'></div>余曰：公之言义之正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274151_comment'></div>不忘渔阳之烈，知尊祖也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274151_comment'></div>不自有濠梁之祥，知尊君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274151_comment'></div>为人后知尊祖，为人臣知尊君，于法当书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274151_comment'></div>余之言义之正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274151_comment'></div>初，淮南被完颜亮之师，公以诸生纠义旅，护乡闾，故安丰不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274151_comment'></div>太上皇帝义而官之，以郡参佐付之，主上又以提封俾镇之，以储阁俾直之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274151_comment'></div>居十有馀年，安丰烟火桑麻，有承平之风焉，又以节俾持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274151_comment'></div>濠梁要地，既归节，又起而俾典之，期年濠梁又成乐国，民无荣悴，地无肥硗，兹惟人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274151_comment'></div>天无心，孰两夫麦之岐，麦无情，孰秀夫岐之两也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274151_comment'></div>有冲气行焉，条达絪缊而为此祥，兹惟人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274151_comment'></div>公于渔阳虽其详未可见，而其人有相似者，为祖若孙，或可以言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274151_comment'></div>渔阳少从世祖，以儒家子为壮夫事，下公孙述于成都，破匈奴、渔阳高柳，以少击众，诸将服之，敌人畏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274151_comment'></div>以健武才施慈祥政，开田畴，劝耕耨，陶富庶于闾阎，能者难之，此与公气象规模，余以为似之，非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274151_comment'></div>渔阳班于郭伋、杜诗、廉范之间，如公则将谁班，议者必有以处之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274151_comment'></div>始公为安丰，有莲一干而两华，及为濠梁，又如之，其祥不独此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274151_comment'></div>然非民政所关，弗著，著其堂所自得名，以示夫有志于育民者观焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1274151_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='81c249efaa674604986860e97b0ab05c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("81c249efaa674604986860e97b0ab05c");'><span id='81c249efaa674604986860e97b0ab05c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>，24岁</div><div id='81c249efaa674604986860e97b0ab05c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月，游湖州东林，作文纪之。作品：《游东林山水记》<div id='poem_1274140' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274140' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274140?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游东林山水记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274140")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274140_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274140'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274140'>绍兴二十八年八月三日欲夕，步自阛阓中出，并溪南行百步，背溪而西又百步，复并溪南行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274140_comment'></div>溪上下色皆重碧幽邃靖深，意若不欲流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274140_comment'></div>溪未穷，得支径，西升上数百尺，既竟其顶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274140_comment'></div>隐而青者，或远在一舍外，锐者如簪，缺者如玦，隆者如髻，圜者如璧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274140_comment'></div>长林远树，出没烟霏，聚者如说，散者如别，整者如戟，乱者如发，于冥濛中以意命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274140_comment'></div>水数百脉，支离轇轕，经纬参错，迤者为溪，漫者为汇，断者为沼，涸者为坳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274140_comment'></div>洲汀岛屿，向背离合，青树碧蔓，交罗蒙络。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274140_comment'></div>小舟叶叶，纵横进退，摘翠者菱，挽红者莲，举白者鱼，或志得意满而归，或夷犹容与若无所为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274140_comment'></div>山有浮图宫，长松数十，挺俨立门左右，历历如流水声，从空中坠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274140_comment'></div>既暮不可留，乃并山北下，冈重岭复，乔木苍苍，月一眉挂修岩巅，迟速若与客俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274140_comment'></div>尽山足，更换二鼓矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274140_comment'></div>翌日又转北，出小桥，并溪东行又西，三四曲折及姚君贵聪门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274140_comment'></div>俯门而航，自柳竹翳密间循渠而出，又三四曲折乃得大溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274140_comment'></div>一色荷花，风自两岸来，红披绿偃，摇荡葳蕤，香气勃郁，冲怀罥袖，掩苒不脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274140_comment'></div>小驻古柳根，得酒两罂，菱芡数种，复引舟入荷花中，歌豪笑剧，响震溪谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274140_comment'></div>风起水面，细生鳞甲，流萤班班，若骇若惊，奄忽去来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274140_comment'></div>夜既深，山益高且近，森森欲下搏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274140_comment'></div>天无一点云，星斗张明，错落水中，如珠走镜，不可收拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274140_comment'></div>隶而从者曰学童，能嘲哳为百鸟音，如行空山深树间，春禽一两声，倏然使人怅而惊也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274140_comment'></div>曰沈庆，能为歌声，回曲宛转，嘹亮激越，风露助之，其声愈清悽然，使人感而悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274140_comment'></div>追游不两朝昏，而东林之胜殆尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274140_comment'></div>同行姚贵聪、沈虞卿、周辅及余四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274140_comment'></div>三君虽纨绮世家，皆积岁忧患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274140_comment'></div>余亦羁旅异乡，家在天西南隅，引领长望而不可归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274140_comment'></div>今而遇此，开口一笑，不偶然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274140_comment'></div>皆应曰：「嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274140_comment'></div>子为之记」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1274140_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>八月，游湖州东林沈氏胜栖堂，作文纪之。作品：《沈氏胜栖堂记》<div id='poem_1274142' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274142' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274142?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沈氏胜栖堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1158年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274142")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274142_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274142'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274142'>余以岁戊寅来东林，此地方为菰田，沈氏兄弟竭智力营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274142_comment'></div>自其先君睥睨十馀年，至是捐金钱数十万，乃得集市之间，民竞辇土石实之，役工数千始平，稍徙花竹藩饰其处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274142_comment'></div>余为指其最胜者，曰：「是可堂，异时果堂，其以『胜栖』名之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274142_comment'></div>二子齐诺，即所指地增筑，将基为堂者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274142_comment'></div>后四年过之，所规为略就，位置行列皆应绳墨，曰：「凡堂之材若资悉具，忌岁未敢屋，以俟明年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274142_comment'></div>又三年过之，芙蓉木犀梅杏桃李皆成林，杨柳冬青皆成荫，修竹满径，菱荷满池，隐然一堂，宏丽靖深，挟以蔽轩，引以修廊，是为胜栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274142_comment'></div>进二子而谓之曰：余过此者三，初过之，地始除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274142_comment'></div>再过之，堂始营；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274142_comment'></div>三过之，草木森然，栋宇穹然，昔意于心，今形于目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274142_comment'></div>二子持家有功，抑余告子：物难于成易毁，事难于进易退，守之在诚，行之在勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274142_comment'></div>子惟肯堂之志甚确，诚守而勤行之，乃克有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274142_comment'></div>先劲后弱，始锐末杀，或隳其中，何成之云？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274142_comment'></div>不辍肯堂，惟堂故成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274142_comment'></div>无斁治身，惟身故立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274142_comment'></div>人情进退甚亟，上之其变三：始而慢，再而骇，三而羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274142_comment'></div>下之其变三：始而疾，再而怜，三而鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274142_comment'></div>是故丘陵贵增，削则寖颓，江河贵盈，缩则寖涸，学问贵益，损则寖荒，道德贵崇，卑则寖微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274142_comment'></div>子以为然，余将示子以方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274142_comment'></div>义重于财，厚义薄财；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274142_comment'></div>德重于势，就德轻势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274142_comment'></div>礼重于物，崇礼卑物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274142_comment'></div>恩重于怨，取恩舍怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274142_comment'></div>今日三过堂而堂之事三变，他日屡见子而子之能屡更，将有信于余言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274142_comment'></div>长字虞卿，次周辅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1274142_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
江陵（江陵府）

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，27岁</div><div id='e234a764f7d64377bbbf2b95cded83ae' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年8月</a>　罢后，入汪澈荆襄幕。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d940680bf8f74c94b0fd9e4817bff5b4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d940680bf8f74c94b0fd9e4817bff5b4");'><span id='d940680bf8f74c94b0fd9e4817bff5b4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年1月</a>　正月，汪澈入朝为参知政事，王质离开汪澈荆襄幕。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='431fb7ed92f14b2aa51942daa9a166c8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("431fb7ed92f14b2aa51942daa9a166c8");'><span id='431fb7ed92f14b2aa51942daa9a166c8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年3月</a>　三月再过荆州，访张孝祥不遇。有诗。作品：《余过荆州张安国已请祠先行》<div id='poem_548846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>余过荆州张安国已请祠先行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548846")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548846'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548846'>心事何曾吐一分，鼓严早已报三声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548846'>元戎十乘公先启，野渡孤舟我自横。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548846'>细看好山须少驻，缓摇柔橹莫多鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548846'>倘能黄鹤楼前见，安得春江尾柁行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548846_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548846'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548846_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1431baab2e7842e1b6648b4257f58843_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1431baab2e7842e1b6648b4257f58843");'><span id='1431baab2e7842e1b6648b4257f58843_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>，27岁</div><div id='1431baab2e7842e1b6648b4257f58843' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过隆中作有诗。作品：《过隆中村》<div id='poem_549110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_549110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/549110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过隆中村</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_549110")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_549110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_549110'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_549110'>当日隆中事，它时渭上悲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_549110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_549110'>出头知几度，弹指不多时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_549110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_549110'>有客吟梁甫，何人表出师。<div id='poem_sentence_2_549110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_549110'>姓庞名蕴者，应笑卧龙儿<span class='inlineComment2'>（同上书卷三五八一引《雪山集》）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_549110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_549110'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_549110_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过隆中作又有词。作品：《八声甘州•读诸葛武侯传》<div id='poem_73006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_73006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/73006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八声甘州<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>读诸葛武侯传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1161年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_73006")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_73006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_73006'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_73006'>过隆中、桑柘倚斜阳，禾黍战悲风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_73006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_73006'>世若无徐庶，更无庞统，沈了英雄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_73006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73006'>本计东荆西益，观变取奇功。<div id='poem_sentence_2_73006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73006'>转尽青天粟，无路能通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73006_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_73006'>他日杂耕渭上，忽一星飞堕，万事成空。<div id='poem_sentence_4_73006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_73006'>使一曹三马，云雨动蛟龙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_73006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_73006'>看璀璨、出师一表，照乾坤、牛斗气常冲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_73006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_73006'>千年后，锦城相吊，遇草堂翁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_73006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_73006'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(73006)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江（江州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2a589f74d6f84f14a0e4cd9b783370f5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2a589f74d6f84f14a0e4cd9b783370f5");'><span id='2a589f74d6f84f14a0e4cd9b783370f5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>，28岁</div><div id='2a589f74d6f84f14a0e4cd9b783370f5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年3月</a>　三月，在江州与友人王阮同游庐山，有文纪之。作品：《玉渊龙记》<div id='poem_1274141' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274141' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274141?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉渊龙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274141")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274141_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274141'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274141'>五老峰于庐山最高，其傍有瀑，如万斛镕银腾空而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274141_comment'></div>山崖峭，峡水盛怒无所输泻，盘旋勃郁，欲迸崖而出，则有巨石如屋，如屏，如车轮，小者犹如釜，如钟磬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274141_comment'></div>水力不能加之，则益横与石相冲相击，如战马，如奔象，其微者犹如斗鸡，如猎犬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274141_comment'></div>水尽锐以争，石极力以拒，相追数里，率未得胜负也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274141_comment'></div>忽山崖横裂，有如物擘而开之，向所谓巨石皆灭没不见，有如物掀而去之，则有平石曼衍数十丈，如几如镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274141_comment'></div>水力稍宽，方肆欲曼流，则石势微洼，掣水力而赴之，尽坠于深潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274141_comment'></div>彼方挟其无穷之怒而纵其不可遏之情，不虞其有洼也，势一就之，不能以自制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274141_comment'></div>方其与石斗也，犹宛转排蹙，未至夫斗落而无以自禁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274141_comment'></div>至是悬奔骤驰，无峥嵘岌嶪者沮之，其势则崩撞冲激，乃始大肆，如奔星，如激矢，如惊鸥，如戏羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274141_comment'></div>其声如疾雷，如震霆，如百万之战声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274141_comment'></div>其飞流溅沫，如急雨，如飞雹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274141_comment'></div>其穷而下者如泼乳，如挥膏，是谓玉渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274141_comment'></div>两崖植立，如铸，如削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274141_comment'></div>其上则水所自落，其下则敷为浅滩，湔为细流，独其中不知其几百万丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274141_comment'></div>相传有龙居之，往往夜静月明，或见有妇人立于潭际者，即之辄入于渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274141_comment'></div>有僧负溪为厕，梦有妇人诃责，安得污我室，比夕再梦，僧惧，亟去之，乃止，故以是为雌龙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274141_comment'></div>夫水惟其无心，至则受之，而玉渊纤芥之触不纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274141_comment'></div>人有负剑浣衣者，剑忽跃去，趣之并没于潭，已而浮尸于潭之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274141_comment'></div>近岁久雨，大水涌至，山石皆突出，空行潭面而过，无一坠者，其为龙居信然不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274141_comment'></div>间雨旸弗若，守土之臣有祷必先焉，无不立应，盖其来久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274141_comment'></div>绍兴三十二年三月十七日，予与友人王阮南卿俱来栖贤访智通，不遇，则徘徊玉渊亭上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274141_comment'></div>有若蛇者骤见于崩涛骇浪之中，或与水曲折相抵冒如钩，或引吭树起如笔，平行见其背如黛，倒侧见其腹如金，蜿蜒上下，如戏如怒，如有所喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274141_comment'></div>予顾谓南卿曰：「是何为者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274141_comment'></div>予疑其非常蛇者二：玉渊之上，去草木甚远，平衍莹滑，非蛇所宜至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274141_comment'></div>且水势乃尔，他蛇至则靡矣，尚安能立？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274141_comment'></div>是二者吾意其龙焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274141_comment'></div>南卿未对，智通自外归，指以问之，智通骇曰：「是矣，是尝出焉，所闻正若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274141_comment'></div>以子岂有所求欤，何为其至也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274141_comment'></div>予曰：「求之而后至，不求则不至矣，则其出没无亦皆关于世欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274141_comment'></div>尔言非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274141_comment'></div>予闻古之见异人与物者，必其真气全也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274141_comment'></div>天地万物皆是气也，是气者全大，而天地夥，而万物皆吾类也，不全则有所隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274141_comment'></div>异物非能神也，有所间断，则若两家者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274141_comment'></div>间断则疏，疏则隐，隐则神矣，而后有异物者生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274141_comment'></div>三代之前，有豢龙氏、御龙氏之官，其豢而御之也，无以异于常畜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274141_comment'></div>彼其天机深而嗜欲浅，其于真气未有所伤也，则见龙也如见夫马牛也，又奚能神？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274141_comment'></div>道丧而人伪滋起，而后鞭策制马，楅衡制牛，于马牛犹所惮，而况于龙乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274141_comment'></div>予之闻道末矣，尝于杭州遇异人焉，以为可与语也，予问其故，曰：『世人委顺流靡者最害于道，何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274141_comment'></div>见物则迁，中无定操也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274141_comment'></div>子刚猛而果锐，有所不为，世外之欲鲜焉，其庶几乎』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274141_comment'></div>兹龙之出，岂不以吾偶有自脱于世尘而近道也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274141_comment'></div>庄子曰：『天地与我并生，万物与我为一』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274141_comment'></div>吾然后知玉渊之为吾囊橐，而兹龙之为吾血属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1274141_comment'></div>尔乃以为求而致之，则往来于玉渊者相踵尔，盍不告之，俾求之欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1274141_comment'></div>智通曰：「唯唯」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1274141_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年10月</a>　是年冬在江州。时张孝祥之父张祁（字晋彦）新任知州，王质代其作谢表。作品：《代张江州谢到任表》<div id='poem_1274083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代张江州谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274083")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274083'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274083'>赋政外台，弗称将明之旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274083_comment'></div>承流支郡，遽膺师帅之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274083_comment'></div>仰大君观过之仁，开小臣自新之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274083_comment'></div>拜命跼蹐，感恩涕洟<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274083_comment'></div>伏念臣学无本根，材有剂量，精神困顿于百忧之后，齿发彫零于多病之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274083_comment'></div>生也有涯，寖迫骎骎之老景；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274083_comment'></div>身其馀几，但存耿耿之壮怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274083_comment'></div>虽一行之尚堪，恐万分之无补，腰佩鱼符之宠，心惭鼠技之穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274083_comment'></div>方九重念彫瘵之民，有如赤子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274083_comment'></div>罄四海尽循良之吏，安用菲材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274083_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下天覆纮埏，海涵动植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274083_comment'></div>怜臣赋命之浅薄，数蹈于网罗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274083_comment'></div>察臣起家之艰难，粗谙于稼穑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274083_comment'></div>爰假列城之守，俾行平日之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274083_comment'></div>臣敢不谨守教条，明宣德意！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274083_comment'></div>必先四者，愿推施仁发政之心，比及三年，傥获有勇知方之效。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1274083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年10月</a>　是年冬在江州。又代张祁作谢张浚启。作品：《代张守谢张都督启》<div id='poem_1274101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代张守谢张都督启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274101")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274101'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274101'>持部使者之权，弗能将命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274101_comment'></div>视古诸侯之秩，遽起为州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274101_comment'></div>悼擢发之罪盈，感嘘枯之德厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274101_comment'></div>伏念某智非语上，才不逮中，曾大道之弗闻，致危机之数蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274101_comment'></div>往堕司刑之密网，实蒙太上之深恩，宽其九死之诛，赐以再生之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274101_comment'></div>用之礼乐，惟难称于光华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274101_comment'></div>畏此简书，粗服劳于奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274101_comment'></div>终坐才疏而意广，弗知福过以灾生，至身挤渊谷之危，殆天夺神明之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274101_comment'></div>置尊拳于鸡肋，何以当之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274101_comment'></div>厝烈火于鸿毛，必无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274101_comment'></div>顾惟么么，安用诛锄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274101_comment'></div>既偶逭于严科，苟自存于馀喘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274101_comment'></div>尘凝满席，秖图饭饱以从容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274101_comment'></div>门设常关，不问客来之剥啄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274101_comment'></div>听苍狗白衣之改变，任双凫乘雁之去来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274101_comment'></div>袖手旁观，已断不谈于世事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274101_comment'></div>缨冠往救，未能绝念于乡邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274101_comment'></div>但虞覆辙之车，几作伤弓之鸟，敢谋更始，犹使治民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274101_comment'></div>惟九江据水陆之冲，当一面受襟喉之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274101_comment'></div>时维东晋，视荆豫以分权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274101_comment'></div>岁纪绍兴，兼舒蕲而授节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274101_comment'></div>岂容重寄，乃付陈人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274101_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官道大无方，功高不伐，充德量以乾坤之广，霈仁恩于河海之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274101_comment'></div>怜不谏之前非，规未来之后效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274101_comment'></div>钦惟旧德，载遇荣期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274101_comment'></div>镃基不如待时，正饥食渴饮之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274101_comment'></div>天地亦各从类，乃风虎云龙之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274101_comment'></div>兼收群才，共集大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274101_comment'></div>自揣不堪于一障，何能有补于万方？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274101_comment'></div>某敢不运甓苦形，饮冰厉志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274101_comment'></div>提封千里，当抚摩凋俗以安居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274101_comment'></div>飞棹百艘，更鼓舞壮夫而效命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1274101_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年10月</a>　是年冬在江州。又有诗与张祁唱和。作品：《和张晋彦》<div id='poem_548708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和张晋彦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1162年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548708")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548708'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548708'>白草蒙荒烟，江南似江北。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548708'>游子无故乡，去住总为客。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548708'>平生不如意，江阔见面窄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548708'>相逢酒一杯，意气感知识。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548708'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548708_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='af43e550332645bd843acf4029f25537_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("af43e550332645bd843acf4029f25537");'><span id='af43e550332645bd843acf4029f25537_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>，33岁</div><div id='af43e550332645bd843acf4029f25537' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>　春，与张孝祥同游庐山。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='299cd40d141049a19da0c039aca3d688_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("299cd40d141049a19da0c039aca3d688");'><span id='299cd40d141049a19da0c039aca3d688_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，29岁</div><div id='299cd40d141049a19da0c039aca3d688' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年1月</a>　正月，至扬州入张浚江淮幕。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='26cfc6ec7b6f426aa7409f9ea3c49163_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("26cfc6ec7b6f426aa7409f9ea3c49163");'><span id='26cfc6ec7b6f426aa7409f9ea3c49163_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，29岁</div><div id='26cfc6ec7b6f426aa7409f9ea3c49163' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年4月</a>　八月，代张浚写谢表。作品：《代张魏公谢表》<div id='poem_1274086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274086?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代张魏公谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274086")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274086'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274086'>授任无方，功垂成而忽败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274086_comment'></div>至仁不杀，罪当死以更生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274086_comment'></div>既苟逭于大刑，仍弗移于故任，彊颜拜命，流涕衔恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274086_comment'></div>伏念臣遭时艰虞，受国光宠，自惜四朝之旧物，尝居百辟之上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274086_comment'></div>意广才疏，乃自天而夙赋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274086_comment'></div>主忧臣辱，实无地以能容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274086_comment'></div>自叨授钺之权，每切系缨之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274086_comment'></div>痛国威之不振，致边警之多虞，誓以三军，决于两阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274086_comment'></div>转石之势，方疾投于千仞之颠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274086_comment'></div>破竹之威，旋见格于数节之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274086_comment'></div>当知难而遂退，乃贪进以不休，众散而归，民逃其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274086_comment'></div>莫解陆沉之愤，益深旰食之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274086_comment'></div>向郊次以哭师，至下行秦伯之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274086_comment'></div>载厨车而徇市，将奚逃汉法之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274086_comment'></div>敢期肉骨之恩，尚诡焚舟之举！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274086_comment'></div>虽回溪失律，他日冀黾池之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274086_comment'></div>然城濮丧军，何颜见申息之老？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274086_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下顺帝之则，与神为谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274086_comment'></div>怜臣耿耿之孤忠，惟知徇国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274086_comment'></div>谅臣区区之小信，尚足使人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274086_comment'></div>遏横议于风波，脱微躯于鼎镬，尽蠲宿负，俾励后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274086_comment'></div>臣敢不蒐揽智能，申明纪律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274086_comment'></div>焚龙庭而犁沙漠，终必望燕然之铭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274086_comment'></div>馘王双而遁郭淮，行且报街亭之辱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1274086_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南陵（宁国府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='11b26385796c4dd4a448e5cb6040cd6e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("11b26385796c4dd4a448e5cb6040cd6e");'><span id='11b26385796c4dd4a448e5cb6040cd6e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>，29岁</div><div id='11b26385796c4dd4a448e5cb6040cd6e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年4月</a>　四月，离扬州至南陵，以沿途见闻、民情报之张浚。作品：《与张都督书》<div id='poem_1274092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与张都督书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1163年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274092")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274092'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274092'>某自四月离扬州，今至南陵，三日而行四百里，劳苦之状不言可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274092_comment'></div>独是阴以观听求诸道涂，荟蕞见闻，或可以补助万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274092_comment'></div>前书略以某人御下无状之迹告之钦夫，持兵劫属官之书，拟刃临总领之舆，纵火焚编民之草，乘酒撞纳妇之居，甚不祥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274092_comment'></div>某在相公左右未尝闻之，某犹不闻也，计不复至于相公之前矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274092_comment'></div>然则相公平日所闻，惧有非其真也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274092_comment'></div>夫居人之上者，下之颦笑屈伸无所不当知之，故能得其隐微而为之潴泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274092_comment'></div>古之为君也，或出入南亩之间，「曾孙来止」是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274092_comment'></div>为吏者或旨否馌食之际，「田畯至喜」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274092_comment'></div>凡为此者，无所不知之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274092_comment'></div>后世之民视君如帝，视大吏如神，视小吏如龙麟虎豹，可见而不可近也，故上之人耳目寝狭而下之人肝肠寖壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274092_comment'></div>幸而达也，未有无所历且无所托而能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274092_comment'></div>对面之间，犹有乖隔，况涉数传之后乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274092_comment'></div>相公之尊，其得见者有数矣，见而敢言、言而敢尽者又有数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274092_comment'></div>故某惟相公平日之所闻有非下情所诚然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274092_comment'></div>古之君子以苦言为良药，以甘言为美疢，何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274092_comment'></div>苦言之多出于情，而甘言之或浮于实也，虽不皆然，要十之八九矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274092_comment'></div>前侍相公，因言赵沂来告吴璘之师复振，西人之归不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274092_comment'></div>近见冯时行移书唐立夫，深病璘而危蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274092_comment'></div>赵子之论是，冯子犹不失忧时爱国之贤者，冯子之论是，赵子可胜罪乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274092_comment'></div>然则，冯子非欺人者也，赵子虽不欺人，为人所欺，则未可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274092_comment'></div>某亦安知某人为能与否，有不令子弟，足见其无贤父兄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274092_comment'></div>然此言难信者，此事非某之素习也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274092_comment'></div>耕织当问奴婢，军旅当问武夫，书生非其业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274092_comment'></div>问佛于僧，其知之固也，至于饮酒茹荤为僧之病者，其徒未有肯自列也，问他人则知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274092_comment'></div>相公重以军旅之事而问士大夫，亦重以士大夫之议而言将帅，岂不以非其业故耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274092_comment'></div>古之豪杰部宾客以军法，是灭秦抗汉之规也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274092_comment'></div>敕儿曹为部曲，是驾魏陵吴之势也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274092_comment'></div>近见陈阜卿云，始谓御军为难，今又措置民兵府卒，乃知不过如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274092_comment'></div>某云天下本无难事，意解便了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274092_comment'></div>然兵非士大夫之所常习，亦非士大夫莫能深知，此物与鬼神造化相通，非庸人所能轻解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274092_comment'></div>故某前书略谓钦夫军旅之权，当使渐入士大夫之手，只陈阜卿、张晋彦之流使居兵间，戈鋋刀槊之下，便有古人之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274092_comment'></div>今数大卒为之，没世不能有美绩也，败坏五家军政，职是数大卒，而又灯灯相传，源源不绝，态度殊不甚远，尚有加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274092_comment'></div>有陈金而置庑者，必无宿城之奔，有素服而殿师者，必无德顺之效，此岂过误哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274092_comment'></div>相公以此知诸将之才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274092_comment'></div>早晚还归庙堂，维新宪度，若不易今日之军政，亦不过今日之武功而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274092_comment'></div>相公之诚通天地而开金石，盖有馀也，然精神寖改于前时，功业未满于初心，徒使相公深悲浩叹之不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274092_comment'></div>前日临分之际，相公忽动山林之兴，退与钦夫道而伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274092_comment'></div>谚云：「指望张三作王大，争奈王大是张三」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274092_comment'></div>蹉跎相公至此者，则此曹为之也，岂独诸将之罪哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274092_comment'></div>张晋彦闻已得祠，必过维扬谒相公，试留与语观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274092_comment'></div>偶动怀抱，不觉宣泄，尚惟钧恕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1274092_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
石泉
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6e2d82cf268f4146b46181180aee2f95_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6e2d82cf268f4146b46181180aee2f95");'><span id='6e2d82cf268f4146b46181180aee2f95_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年</a>，33岁</div><div id='6e2d82cf268f4146b46181180aee2f95' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年10月</a>　九、十月间，途经利州东路石泉县饶风岭时，有词。作品：《水调歌头（饶风岭上见梅）》<div id='poem_73015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_73015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/73015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_73015")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_73015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_73015'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_73015'>草蔓已多露，松竹总含风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_73015'>群山左顾右盼，如虎更如龙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73015'>时见渔灯三两，知在谁家浦溆，星斗烂垂空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73015'>万有付一扫，人世等天宫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73015_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_73015'>秋萧瑟，林脱叶，水归洪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_73015'>江湖飘泊鸿雁，洲渚肯相容。<div id='poem_sentence_5_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_73015'>要使群生安堵，不听三更吠犬，此则是奇功。<div id='poem_sentence_6_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_73015'>一任画麟阁，吾自老墙东。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_73015_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
汉中（兴元府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='19b44a8dc1ce4be88f8e8efdca98fd9d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("19b44a8dc1ce4be88f8e8efdca98fd9d");'><span id='19b44a8dc1ce4be88f8e8efdca98fd9d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1168')">1167-1168年</a>，33-34岁</div><div id='19b44a8dc1ce4be88f8e8efdca98fd9d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年10月25日</a>　十月二十五日到达利州后，有词。作品：《定风波（赠将）》<div id='poem_73038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_73038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/73038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>定风波<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_73038")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_73038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_73038'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_73038'>白璧黄金爵上卿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_73038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_73038'>紫宸殿下拜丝纶。<div id='poem_sentence_1_73038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73038'>才出龙门开虎帐，但看，甲光如水夜无尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_73038_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73038'>古古今今男子事，摇动，芙蓉旗影入金樽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_73038'>到得关河公事了，早去，白云堆里养精神。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_73038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月2日</a>　十一月，虞允文生日，作寿雅致贺。作品：《枢相宣抚虞公寿雅并序》<div id='poem_548697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>枢相宣抚虞公寿雅<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>汉清</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年11月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548697")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548697'>汉水之清，其石粼粼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548697'>仁寿公来思，汉水则清。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_1_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548697'>汉水之浊<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作蜀，据孔本，秦本改）</span>，其洄澳澳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548697'>仁寿公往思，汉水则浊。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548697'>农耰于野，不蹂一苗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548697'>贾驰于郊，不惊一毛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548697'>公在襄阳，民生逍遥。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_6_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548697'>公来自东，襄民蹙蹙，止公毋西。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_7_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548697'>公来自吴，襄民蹙蹙，止公毋蜀。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_8_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548697'>金我襄城，汤我汉江。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548697'>春我之筐，秋我之箱。<span class='charType'>（六章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_10_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_548697'>我耄皤皤，公昔年<span class='inlineComment2'>（孔本作言）</span>之，而曷捐之。<span class='charType'>（七章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_548697'>我孩婴婴，公昔体之，而曷置之。<span class='charType'>（八章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_12_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_548697'>日月躞躞，勿黧公色。<div id='poem_sentence_13_548697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_548697'>霜露烈烈，勿华公发。<span class='charType'>（九章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_14_548697_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_548697'>公发勿华，我生则遐。<div id='poem_sentence_15_548697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_548697'>吁彼苍天，佑我皇家。<span class='charType'>（十章）</span><br /></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_548697_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548698' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548698' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548698?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>江舻</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年11月2日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548698_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548698'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548698'>江之沄沄，舻之贲贲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548698'>敌之休休，震于昆崙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548698'>仁寿公一临，靡靡其倾。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_2_548698_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548698'>江之洋洋，舻之扬扬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548698'>敌之煌煌，孔炽厥芒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548698'>仁寿公一嘘，萧萧其凉。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_5_548698_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548698'>天子在宫，有恫悒悒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548698'>神主在庙，有震岌岌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548698'>暨我国人，以莫不惕。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_8_548698_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548698'>在宫雍雍，金石其音。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548698'>在庙湛湛，虎兕其扃。<div id='poem_sentence_10_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_548698'>暨我国人，以莫不宁。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_548698_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_548698'>有庚之寅，维公其生。<div id='poem_sentence_12_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_548698'>在巳之辛，维公其成。<div id='poem_sentence_13_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_548698'>而有斯厄，而有斯人。<div id='poem_sentence_14_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_548698'>匪天之私，伊宋之仁。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_15_548698_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_548698'>大江之滨，采石之津。<div id='poem_sentence_16_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_548698'>波之沦沦，石之粼粼。<div id='poem_sentence_17_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_548698'>谓公可堙，江则可尘。<div id='poem_sentence_18_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_548698'>山之嵚嵚，隰之畇畇。<div id='poem_sentence_19_548698_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_548698'>谓公可磨，山则可簪。<span class='charType'>（六章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_20_548698_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_548698'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_548698_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年11月2日</a>　十一月冬雷，代虞允文作待罪表。作品：《代虞丞相冬雷待罪表》<div id='poem_1274088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代虞丞相冬雷待罪表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年11月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274088")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274088_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274088'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274088'>闭藏之月，雷乃发声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274088_comment'></div>辅佐之司，义难逃责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274088_comment'></div>伏念臣推移至此，经济蔑然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274088_comment'></div>在二三臣之间，才最居于下乘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274088_comment'></div>越数千里之外，位犹玷于元枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274088_comment'></div>难使处中之臣，独当弗若之咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274088_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下上承天意，下酌民言，责其无补于朝廷，正以有常之刑典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274088_comment'></div>盖《坎》《离》易位，是岂为标末之灾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274088_comment'></div>虽天地至仁，不敢望函容之造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1274088_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年3月</a>　在虞允文川陕幕。六月上启制置使晁公武。作品：《上晁制置启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱系六月，误。晁公武三月获任命，其时在兴元府，王质亦在兴元府。）</span><div id='poem_1274102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上晁制置启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274102")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274102'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274102'>十年而受坎𡒄，殊无宦情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274102_comment'></div>一旦而得依归，顿有生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274102_comment'></div>以半生之齿发，与百指之妻孥，寘在并包之中，托为生死之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274102_comment'></div>某之平素，公所照知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274102_comment'></div>无内美与修能，有灵均与正则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274102_comment'></div>日遒尽而羲和不容于弭节，路曼修而望舒不亟于先驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274102_comment'></div>伏念某神交吴下之一书，心醉汉中之数面，以此决策，翻然委身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274102_comment'></div>恭惟某官纲维鼓舞之神，而应以无方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274102_comment'></div>负荷英豪之气，而御之有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274102_comment'></div>宏知驰骛于鬼神天地之表，博学经纬于帝霸皇王之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274102_comment'></div>三代有其人，至秦、汉而不闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274102_comment'></div>六经有其事，更荀、扬而弗著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274102_comment'></div>岂谓当代，乃生斯贤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274102_comment'></div>虽祖宗积累之使然，亦期运推移之至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274102_comment'></div>顾两宫未满之愿，与四海同然之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274102_comment'></div>有大功名，终落公手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274102_comment'></div>凡今人物，谁同此心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274102_comment'></div>傥不鄙夷，愿相料理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274102_comment'></div>恐事于此去矣，庾征西至迫殷浩以见从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274102_comment'></div>其肯为我来乎，乌大夫犹虑石洪之不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274102_comment'></div>凡今日全家而求托，盖平时慕义以来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274102_comment'></div>惟所控提，以之奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274102_comment'></div>颇有如此客，固未足以满怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274102_comment'></div>乃能驾驭卿，亦何患于无势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274102_comment'></div>行将敛板，豫达空函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274102_comment'></div>逢迎有主人，都无遗恨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274102_comment'></div>跪起如子侄，曷敢不恭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274102_comment'></div>南楼夜月之据床，北地秋风之分楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274102_comment'></div>老子有兴之际，痴儿了事之馀，咏红莲绿水之风流，望黄色赤云之气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274102_comment'></div>容司马之狂于方外，敢以此施于严尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274102_comment'></div>志书记之名于壁间，庶来者得以观览。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1274102_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年3月</a>　在虞允文川陕幕。六月虞允文宴请晁公武，代虞允文作诗唱和。作品：《代虞枢密宴晁制置口号二首》<div id='poem_548835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代虞枢密宴晁制置口号二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_548835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548835'>合奏元和鼓吹声，旌幢交映两辕门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548835'>中台上相官仪重，大国诸侯礼数尊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548835'>一会星辰朝北极，八方风雨聚西坤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548835'>今朝宾主周旋地，千古英豪气象昏。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548836?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1168年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548836'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_73015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_73015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/73015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1167年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", id='poem_sentence_0_73015'>草蔓已多露，松竹总含风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_73015'>群山左顾右盼，如虎更如龙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73015'>时见渔灯三两，知在谁家浦溆，星斗烂垂空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73015'>万有付一扫，人世等天宫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73015_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_73015'>秋萧瑟，林脱叶，水归洪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_73015'>江湖飘泊鸿雁，洲渚肯相容。<div id='poem_sentence_5_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_73015'>要使群生安堵，不听三更吠犬，此则是奇功。<div id='poem_sentence_6_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_73015'>一任画麟阁，吾自老墙东。</div><div class='inlineComment2'>（同题诗有两首，卷十三为五律，卷十五为七绝。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年11月4日</a>　十一月四日，随虞允文到成都。<br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年</a>　在利州期间，还有诗。作品：《和御制诗五首》<div id='poem_548753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548753_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_548753_0'>① 原案：此诗当是孝宗乾道三四年间所作。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548753'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548753'>列圣兼仁武，随时议战和。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73068'>吴江虽有晚潮回。未比合江亭下、水如飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年5月</a>　在蜀期间，有诗。作品：《题观政池桥》《游杨氏园》<div id='poem_548724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548724?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题观政池桥<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548724")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_548724_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_548724_0'>① 原案：此诗及《游杨氏园》诗，当是孝宗乾道四年六年质在蜀时所作。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548724'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548724'>西彻秦川东剑关，十有六州无间言。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548724'>威声浩荡流东南，与大江水同发源。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548724'>节麾毵毵绣衣鲜，刚风吹上九天门。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548724'>手从瑶宫掇明月，贮在官池水不浑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548724'>菱叶荷花净晼晚，舂锄属玉来频烦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_548724'>冷光烈烈射地骨，魑魅辟易声烦冤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_548724'>牛腰抱去凫行速，来瞰皎洁听潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548724'>玉龙蟠底抱奇宝，獠奴试可呼昆崙。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548724'>洞庭青草似天阔，滟滪瞿唐如马奔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548724'>不如我池有幽致，宝奁平开秋露洗。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548724'>高人未到已神融，俗客若来应颡泚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_548724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_548724'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_548724_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548725' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548725' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548725?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_548725'>幽芳秀阴似琅琊，三四牛鸣通浣花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548725'>少陵醉卧元不死，强请起来殊更佳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548725'>向来娟娟隔秋水，谁与为期同在此。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548725'>德星分野到杨家，亦有致然非偶尔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548725'>萧萧骚骚诗韵寒，腷腷膊膊棋声乾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548725'>是日成都极炎热，此堂阴风下浓雪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_548725'>谈端天地不支吾，笔下龙蛇争撇挒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_548725'>所恨江南在天末，隔天鸿雁难同飞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_548725'>彭蠡洞庭隔烟水，他日岂不怀此时。<div id='poem_sentence_9_548725_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_548725'>他日安得如此时，杨家壁上更重题。<div id='poem_sentence_1_549104'>斗转参横无定舍，侍郎行处亦随行<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_549104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_549104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_549104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_549104'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_549104_0'>⑴ -----title
奉节
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf4eeeaf7e394622af5481d0f3be5daf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf4eeeaf7e394622af5481d0f3be5daf");'><span id='bf4eeeaf7e394622af5481d0f3be5daf_link' id='poem_sentence_1_73015'>群山左顾右盼，如虎更如龙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_73015'>时见渔灯三两，知在谁家浦溆，星斗烂垂空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_73015'>万有付一扫，人世等天宫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_73015_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_73015'>秋萧瑟，林脱叶，水归洪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_73015'>江湖飘泊鸿雁，洲渚肯相容。<div id='poem_sentence_5_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_73015'>要使群生安堵，不听三更吠犬，此则是奇功。<div id='poem_sentence_6_73015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
