href='/Writing/1274149?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白帝庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274149")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274149'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274149'>白帝公孙氏，茂陵其里也，清水、导江、临邛其生所历也，成都其称帝王及死所也，瞿唐其庙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274149_comment'></div>其庙不知其所始，而其事则可次而言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274149_comment'></div>更始元年称辅汉将军于成都，欲保郡自守以待真主，此白帝素志也，美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274149_comment'></div>二年拒更始所遣将李宝、张忠而称蜀主，贰于汉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274149_comment'></div>当是时世祖皇帝转侧河朔之间未兴，而更始之政已乱，非贰于汉也，贰于更始也，犹之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274149_comment'></div>建武元年，以成家为号而称天子，于是欲与世祖争天下，尚奚言素志，尽反矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274149_comment'></div>白帝其知天命所归否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274149_comment'></div>白帝初闻李熊之言，辞曰：「帝王有命，吾何足以当之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274149_comment'></div>白帝之知审也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274149_comment'></div>熊曰：「天命无常，百姓与能，能者当之，又何疑焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274149_comment'></div>熊之弗知，非白帝之弗知，又审也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274149_comment'></div>误白帝者熊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274149_comment'></div>六年，世祖腾书为白帝平素之言，且曰：「天下神器不可以力争」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274149_comment'></div>白帝其知神器可争否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274149_comment'></div>是岁隗嚣以陇西归白帝，白帝得之，与合从拒世祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274149_comment'></div>误白帝者又嚣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274149_comment'></div>嚣不能误窦融而误白帝，窦以兴，公孙以亡，其白帝之不幸非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274149_comment'></div>十二年世祖又移书为白帝苦陈之，且曰：「以时自诣则全」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274149_comment'></div>当是时隗氏灭，任满、田戎败，公孙恢、史兴又败，谢丰、袁吉又败，王师既守成都，白帝其知事势之去否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274149_comment'></div>十二之期至矣，白帝固自知之，而延岑之言曰：「男子当死中求生，可坐穷乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274149_comment'></div>误白帝者又岑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274149_comment'></div>方事之急也，张隆、常少劝白帝以来归，此刘禅之谯周也，而白帝之言曰：「废兴命也，岂有降天子哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274149_comment'></div>则已入岑言于先，隆、少忠谋格矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274149_comment'></div>岑存而隆、少死，何哀如之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274149_comment'></div>使白帝如世祖指挈图迎降，保族安民，与河西窦融同功，智士之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274149_comment'></div>既不能然，势尽力穷，健决糜于一死，不肯为姚泓、慕容超以肉委人，壮士之风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274149_comment'></div>泓之果顾不及其童儿，白帝视之壮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274149_comment'></div>智士之事不足，壮夫之风有馀，庙以祀之，非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274149_comment'></div>蜀也者魏取刘，晋取李、取谯，唐取王，特易于他邦，而汉取公孙最后于馀敌，且难白帝之能高，非禅、势、纵、衍之伦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274149_comment'></div>岑彭、来歙强对也，白帝能间陨之，刘尚败，吴汉危不得脱，白帝之能诚高也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274149_comment'></div>议白帝者难乎其辞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274149_comment'></div>吾以为白帝之祸造于熊，集于嚣，厚于岑，非白帝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274149_comment'></div>如是，其可以少慰白帝之心，不与张步、秦丰同羞，否耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274149_comment'></div>白帝死而为神，据江山之会，而护持往来于险阻之中，丰功茂泽，咸交赞以为归，则泥首衔玉、畏死偷生之流何以得此也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274149_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1274149_comment'></div>其可书也已，其可书也已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1274149_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
武汉
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7566a16d7ce841c4b19ecc851ca3aa71_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7566a16d7ce841c4b19ecc851ca3aa71");'><span id='7566a16d7ce841c4b19ecc851ca3aa71_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，35岁</div><div id='7566a16d7ce841c4b19ecc851ca3aa71' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>三月，上启参知政事、四川宣抚使王炎。作品：《上王参政启》<div id='poem_1274105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上王参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274105")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274105'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274105'>南极一星，历荆扬而西上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274105_comment'></div>长城万里，护江汉以东流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274105_comment'></div>冠两班文武之崇，分万乘旌旗之半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274105_comment'></div>翻路朝之显册，卿士从而大同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274105_comment'></div>灼太庙之元龟，鬼神依而协吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274105_comment'></div>时际君臣之会，情均骨肉之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274105_comment'></div>二人同心，洽金兰之契；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274105_comment'></div>一日不见，觉岁月之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274105_comment'></div>暂命往釐，亶非得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274105_comment'></div>大禹征苗之役未几，而伯益已赞其班师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274105_comment'></div>仲山徂齐之行无何，而吉甫式遄其归觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274105_comment'></div>想二臣濡辔驱驰之际，使两君驰神寤寐之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274105_comment'></div>钦惟列圣之相承，益重大臣之出使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274105_comment'></div>文潞公之帅河北，及阙下亦正大昭文之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274105_comment'></div>韩康公之莅陕西，即军中而颁左仆射之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274105_comment'></div>于皇太上，既及今王，亦遵令猷，以待元老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274105_comment'></div>忠献张公之至，即次赵公而秉钧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274105_comment'></div>仁寿虞公之还，行与陈公而并位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274105_comment'></div>公居此地，前有成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274105_comment'></div>恭惟某官以伊尹之一德而阐幽，以周公之多才而应变，照临四海以羲仲之日，鼓舞万物以老子之龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274105_comment'></div>多历年所而回翔，不终日间而契悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274105_comment'></div>我见魏徵，自比于匠之砺金；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274105_comment'></div>孤有孔明，不啻如鱼之得水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274105_comment'></div>山云之出有开必先，谷风之生同声相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274105_comment'></div>五百年必兴王者，有名世焉而居其间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274105_comment'></div>九五爻利见大人，有亲上者而从其类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274105_comment'></div>尽关天数，非出人谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274105_comment'></div>总二火以制名，符国家之运气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274105_comment'></div>赋一壬而定命，合主上之天元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274105_comment'></div>上帝赉之以泽生灵，圣祖遗之以贻孙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274105_comment'></div>恢洪百度，疆理四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274105_comment'></div>文法技巧之精，有黄龙之象；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274105_comment'></div>车马器械之备，有东都之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274105_comment'></div>忽千载一时之相逢，将三光五岳之复合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274105_comment'></div>祖宗有训，宰相当用北人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274105_comment'></div>周汉以来，太平多从西起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274105_comment'></div>惟桑梓之名邦曰相，而衮绣之先达有韩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274105_comment'></div>载生我公，益懋其美，实河朔英豪之彦，有雍梁形势之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274105_comment'></div>人与地以相当，古至今而莫并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274105_comment'></div>渭上杂耕之志，既格于前代；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274105_comment'></div>富平大举之谋，复隳于近时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274105_comment'></div>留此功名，付公掌握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274105_comment'></div>刘当兴而李为辅，时将至则人随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1274105_comment'></div>来秦易并而羽可图，谋既定则事从以济，才睹行台之建，即知昌运之开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1274105_comment'></div>盍使孤生，预观盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1274105_comment'></div>岂无他人，不如同姓，偶受氏列宗盟之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1274105_comment'></div>既见君子，实获我心，愿终身依门墙之下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1274105_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>又代虞允文作启通报王炎。作品：《代通王制置启》<div id='poem_1274100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代通王制置启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274100")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274100'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274100'>奠坤轴于西维，蔼著金城之誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274100_comment'></div>奉云章于北阙，遄归玉笋之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274100_comment'></div>停鹢首于江干，望斗标于天末，双鲤惊传于尺素，五云喜近于三台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274100_comment'></div>恭惟某官千载伟人，万夫重望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274100_comment'></div>大圭不琢，质涵天地之纯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274100_comment'></div>黄钟为宫，气韫阴阳之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274100_comment'></div>文彩步汉唐之上，风流及晋宋之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274100_comment'></div>峙冰玉于螭坳，见之属目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274100_comment'></div>演丝纶于凤闼，闻者动心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274100_comment'></div>四方于申伯之宣，九命作周官之牧，幅员万里，欢喜一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274100_comment'></div>身留玉垒之偏，声彻剑关之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274100_comment'></div>版图尽入，见黄河天上之源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274100_comment'></div>钲鼓不惊，下滴博云间之戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274100_comment'></div>总蜀部才几于再闰，兼武侯仅数于两人，尚韬游刃之馀，未及叩囊之底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274100_comment'></div>戎行小驻，镇昆崙万国之西；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274100_comment'></div>册拜殊荣，将特进群公之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274100_comment'></div>某久沦潮海，绝望盛明，偶叨半竹之分符，适际介圭之入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274100_comment'></div>见紫芝之眉宇，昔尝睹于英资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274100_comment'></div>望芙蓉之旌旗，今再逢于仙驭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1274100_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>与王炎有诗唱和。作品：《上王公明寿四首》<div id='poem_548774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上王公明寿四首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_548774")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548774_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_548774_0'>① 原案：王公明名炎，为四川宣抚使，此诗当是乾道七年所作。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548774'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548774'>缑氏吹箫远，王家奕叶光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548774'>昔多称建业，今独盛安阳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548774'>泰华何曾老，江河各自长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548774'>一名重两火，与宋大休祥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548774'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548774_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548775?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548775_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548775'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548775'>正统承周后，元臣在邺昌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548775'>治平扶嗣圣，乾道作<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>兴王。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548775'>指日恢中土，何时过故乡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548775'>新堂标昼锦，门下有欧阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548775'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548775_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_548775'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_548775_0'>⑴ 原作乾作道，据孔本、秦本乙</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_548775_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_548776' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548776' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548776?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548776_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548776'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548776'>稷契伊周后，功名事业谁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548776'>眼惊希世杰，心喜太平时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548776'>不老池边凤，长生印上龟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548776'>旂常书不尽，太庙有宗彝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548776'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548776_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_548777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_548777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/548777?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_548777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_548777'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_548777'>风起云飞志，包含具善邻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_548777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_548777'>试看公出手，毋谓我无人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_548777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_548777'>挥羽思平魏，登场决并秦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_548777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_548777'>功成身莫退，小驻八千春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_548777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_548777'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_548777_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
涪陵
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0e9f3c648a7e4c87b9427262dcd4bda1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e9f3c648a7e4c87b9427262dcd4bda1");'><span id='0e9f3c648a7e4c87b9427262dcd4bda1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>，36岁</div><div id='0e9f3c648a7e4c87b9427262dcd4bda1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年6月</a>　过涪陵，谯先生祠，有记文。作品：《涪陵谯先生祠记》<div id='poem_1274148' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274148' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274148?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涪陵谯先生祠记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274148")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274148_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274148'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274148'>孔氏亡而书存，世以其书诱士以为使，外骛之徒利之，故正学废而俗学兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274148_comment'></div>其所资者章句言语、形名度数，豪杰之士不堪以其高明广大之体滞于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274148_comment'></div>佛氏之子有达磨者自西土来中国，断拘挛之见，扫凝滞之具，引学者以骏利之途，天下豪杰相咏赞以为依归，于是佛力始重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274148_comment'></div>自达磨建此宗，而豪杰或见其趣嘘呵踧踏惊绝超拔之功，故豪杰归则权在佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274148_comment'></div>而儒者行世多为富贵威武所制，功业名誉所役，有得于佛氏之家者轻之，儒者虽外不服而内自愧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274148_comment'></div>普通以来，天下以明心见性之捷，非求诸佛氏之门不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274148_comment'></div>吾道之妙布列于《诗》、《书》、《礼》、《乐》，而潜寓于《易》，时出于《论语》《孟子》，而会见于《大学》、《中庸》，未有指而出之，收天下豪杰而归吾宗，故惠能、道一、怀逊、义元之流不受衣冠之所维絷，使吾宗得此百倍于郑玄马融，失之哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274148_comment'></div>伊川先生实始标呈孔氏之秘，比佛氏所明益显露，且亲戚不绝，衣服饮食不易，发奇伟之事于经常之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274148_comment'></div>天下豪杰自有天渊为飞跃之地，异时插锹系竹，咸为吾宗之归，孔氏之权重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274148_comment'></div>涪陵谯先生初习佛，伊川授其学以《大学》、《中庸》而指其法以敬，先生悦之，弃家破产，疲曳妻子以从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274148_comment'></div>及其困饥且死，不以非义之粟而易将殒之命，非天下之豪杰其能建立如此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274148_comment'></div>往余在都，有不悦伊川之学者为余道之，余曰：「建炎之初，诏起谯先生于河南，无所踪迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274148_comment'></div>有野人道使者入嵩山深绝，见先生卧土屋，衣襦，釜灶皆尘，强掖起之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274148_comment'></div>既至，与宰相不合，遂去，不知所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274148_comment'></div>此孔氏所谓遁世无闷，乐则行之，忧则违之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1274148", 1274148, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>确乎</span>其不可拔，潜龙也，天地造化有不可羁绁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274148_comment'></div>或摄受之无难，可谓有力，非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274148_comment'></div>制伏虎豹，非西方狮子不能，他非余所知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274148_comment'></div>是时尚未熟知先生之详，后数年过涪陵见伊川之孙太守程公，示余以武夷胡公宪、河南郭公雍诸文，且道所未尽者，乃得其本末出处甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274148_comment'></div>初，涪陵未有先生祠堂，公至始克为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274148_comment'></div>险远幽仄，有此足以重天下，而无与扬之至今，盖其后徙于伊洛而转仄于吴楚，存没皆不关于故乡，其疏固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274148_comment'></div>虽于先生无所为亏，而乡党之典与牧守之职则为旷，非公道问学敦教化，念其祖而欲崇其徒，奖其先贤而欲风厉其后来者，谁与领此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274148_comment'></div>堂成而余来，非平时有慕于其中而窃见其馀末，又谁当言之，此岂偶然乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274148_comment'></div>先生名定，字天授，起布衣为通直郎、直秘阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274148_comment'></div>丧乱莫知所终，或云终于嵩山少林寺，又云隐居青城之老人村，易姓，迨其今犹存云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1274148_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
云阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cdf3a5f2988742679981f13638cbdfb9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cdf3a5f2988742679981f13638cbdfb9");'><span id='cdf3a5f2988742679981f13638cbdfb9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>，36岁</div><div id='cdf3a5f2988742679981f13638cbdfb9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年6月</a>　过云安，拜谒张飞庙，有记。作品：《张益德庙记》<div id='poem_1274150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1274150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1274150?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张益德庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1170年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30344, "南宋", "王质", "poem_title_1274150")'>王质</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1274150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1274150'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1274150'>汉车骑将军、领司隶校尉、西乡侯张公，与诸葛武侯、关氏壮侯，以文武相济，夹辅先主，绍延汉基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1274150_comment'></div>其子孙终始死生之际，皆无负汉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1274150_comment'></div>天以此三人遗先主成邦而共为存亡，所谓期运者非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1274150_comment'></div>初，先主与公同以涿郡为乡，先得公，壮侯自解奔涿，于是乃得壮侯，皆燕南故人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1274150_comment'></div>及先主依刘表驻新野，于是乃得武侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1274150_comment'></div>语序武侯新于二公，而先主所为鱼水者在武侯惟深，此二公所以弗悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1274150_comment'></div>虽其迹如此，而忠于汉则三公同一心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1274150_comment'></div>公之孙尚书遵、武侯之子卫将军瞻俱死事于绵竹，壮侯之孙寿亭侯彝与其宗歼于成都，所谓共为存亡者非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1274150_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1274150_comment'></div>事将成天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1274150_comment'></div>初，先主畏偪，自樊略宛，循襄阳向江陵，至当阳之长坂，曹公垂将及之，危哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1274150_comment'></div>公据水断桥，瞋目横矛，以二十骑遏数十万之师不得前，而先主得斜道趋汉津，会壮侯舟师以脱，其不死幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1274150_comment'></div>于是武侯以大计说孙公，而周瑜赤壁之事乃济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1274150_comment'></div>败曹公也，其人为周瑜，天下户知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1274150_comment'></div>说孙公也，其人为武侯，天下亦户知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1274150_comment'></div>以舟师济先主也，其人为壮侯，天下亦户知之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1274150_comment'></div>至断桥却敌，以免先主，未有明为高于他功者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1274150_comment'></div>微公，先主齑粉矣，武侯、壮侯安在哉，而尚赤壁耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1274150_comment'></div>此汉事之将成，天遗公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1274150_comment'></div>呜呼，事不成亦天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1274150_comment'></div>初，先主锐复壮侯之雠，是以为吴之师，公提万数之旅顺流而东下，陆逊岂易当之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1274150_comment'></div>哀哉，阆之难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1274150_comment'></div>公死而张南、冯习本兵，猇亭、秭归之耻，童子知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1274150_comment'></div>此汉事之不成，天夺公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1274150_comment'></div>天将坏人家国，先夺其人，人亡而后家国从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1274150_comment'></div>台城陷，羊侃先死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1274150_comment'></div>江陵陷，胡僧祐先死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1274150_comment'></div>汴州陷，王彦章先死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1274150_comment'></div>寿春陷，刘仁瞻先死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1274150_comment'></div>人弗死，如基弗摧，室弗倾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1274150_comment'></div>夫先主北向以争天下，中道而失壮侯，实建安二十四年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1274150_comment'></div>东向以争江南，中道而失公，实章武元年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1274150_comment'></div>不二年无两公，先主身老志彫，而永安之变已矣，天其可知也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1274150_comment'></div>武侯上失先主，下失两公，而黄忠之卒以壮侯死之明年，马超之卒以公死之明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1274150_comment'></div>异哉，其参会也，汉之羽翼殄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1274150_comment'></div>武侯欲以杨仪、魏延、李严、马谡之辈而回天心，武侯非不知之，其「未解」之条六章可以推之矣，至「鞠躬尽力，死而后已，其成败利钝非能逆睹」，此武侯平生大指而形诸辞者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1274150_comment'></div>后十三年而武侯死，汉事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1274150_comment'></div>公不没于阆，壮侯不没于临沮，而武侯犹未殡于渭原，殆未可量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1274150_comment'></div>公自中平之初至建安之末，事先主凡三十有八年，其相先后而终才一年有奇，废兴存没，其果有数也，非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1274150_comment'></div>公既没而为神，其丰功茂泽形于死者愈益加于生，则公为不死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1274150_comment'></div>神仙不死以气之贞，豪杰不死以气之英，气无间于穷壤，无隔于今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1274150_comment'></div>呜呼，其可以弗敬也夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1274150_comment'></div>其可以弗敬也夫！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1274150_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
鄂城（武昌）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d0bf32c5ebdb441fabe28483bfe68768_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d0bf32c5ebdb441fabe28483bfe68768");'><span id='d0bf32c5ebdb441fabe28483bfe68768_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>，36岁</div><div id='d0bf32c5ebdb441fabe28483bfe68768' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年7月20日</a>　七月二十日到武昌，有书信寄虞允文。作品：《与虞相书》（一）<br /></div>
-----end
